Education News

Important News 92

Student Representatives

Cannot Participate in School Affairs Meetings

The Ministry of Education, based on the inquiry from the president of the private Great China University regarding whether student representatives from the school can participate in the university affairs council, specifically instructed the school, stating: "Received. The organizational personnel of the university affairs meeting have been clearly stipulated in Article 15 of the University Organization Law promulgated by the National Government, and there are no student representatives included. Furthermore, Article 15 of the central resolution on the organization outline of student self-government states that student self-government associations must not interfere with school administration. It is clear that representatives of student organizations must not participate in school affairs meetings. Please comply accordingly. Furthermore, the name of the university affairs meeting in your report does not comply with the name stipulated in the University Organization regulations and should be corrected immediately."

Overseas Chinese School 93

Relief Measures for Issuing School Seals

The Ministry of Education, based on the report from Guangdong Education Department Director Xu Chongqing, stated that the Overseas Chinese Private Yuqun Elementary School in the Mian Gong province of French Annam has submitted school registration forms and seal fees, requesting registration and issuance of school seals. Before investigating where overseas Chinese schools should issue school seals, the various elementary schools established by Overseas Chinese in Annam, Guangdong, have submitted requests for the issuance of school seals, which have been reported to the Ministry for instructions, but no approval has been received. Now, the previous situation is reported again, and it is appropriate to prepare a document to request the Ministry to examine and instruct, etc. The Ministry of Education issued an instruction stating, "Received. The Overseas Chinese Education Conference convened by the Central Training Department last November discussed measures regarding the governing institutions of Overseas Chinese schools. However, before they are announced, school seals for Overseas Chinese schools in places where there are no consuls can be temporarily issued by the provincial education department that is geographically closer. The schools mentioned in the report, all levels of schools established by Overseas Chinese in Annam and Guangdong, should submit requests for the issuance of school seals to the respective provincial education departments. You are hereby ordered to acknowledge and instruct accordingly."

Boy Scout Headquarters Promulgates Various Regulations 94

(3) Organizational Regulations of the China Boy Scout Special Municipality Council

Article 1: In special municipalities where seven or more China Boy Scout troops have been established, the training department of the special municipality's party headquarters may petition the China Boy Scout Headquarters to organize a China Boy Scout special municipality council, named the China Boy Scout [Name of Special Municipality] Council, to execute the orders of the China Boy Scout Headquarters and handle matters such as the organization, guidance, and assessment of local Boy Scouts.

Article 2: The China Boy Scout Special Municipality Council shall be organized by five to seven directors and three alternate directors. The director of the training department of the local party headquarters and the director of the education bureau shall be ex officio directors. The remaining directors shall be mutually elected by local Boy Scout service members every six months and appointed by the China Boy Scout Headquarters upon approval by the training department of the special municipality's party headquarters.

Article 3: The China Boy Scout Special Municipality Council shall have three executive directors, who shall be mutually elected by the directors to organize an executive meeting to handle daily affairs.

Article 4: The China Boy Scout Special Municipality Council shall have a secretary who shall execute council affairs under the guidance of the executive directors.

Article 5: The China Boy Scout Special Municipality Council may establish four sections based on the complexity of the affairs: organization, guidance, assessment, and general affairs. Each section shall have a chief secretary and several secretaries and clerks, who shall manage the affairs of each section and draft documents under the guidance of the executive directors and the secretary. The aforementioned chief secretaries and secretaries shall be concurrently appointed by personnel transferred from agencies or organizations related to the Boy Scout cause and shall not be paid.

Article 6: The detailed rules of procedure for the China Boy Scout Special Municipality Council shall be drafted by the council and submitted to the China Boy Scout Commander for approval.

Article 7: Any matters not covered in these regulations shall be amended by the Central Executive Committee upon submission by the China Boy Scout Commander.

Article 8: These regulations shall be implemented upon approval by the Standing Committee of the Central Executive Committee after submission by the China Boy Scout Commander.

(4) Organizational Regulations of the China Boy Scout County (City) Council 95

Article 1: In counties or cities where five or more China Boy Scout troops have been established, the training department of the county or city party headquarters may petition the China Boy Scout Provincial Council to forward the request to the China Boy Scout Commander to organize a China Boy Scout county or city council, named the China Boy Scout [Name of Province] [Name of County/City] Council, to execute the orders of the Provincial Council and handle matters such as the organization, guidance, and assessment of local Boy Scouts. However, if the Provincial Council has not been established, the petition may be submitted directly to the China Boy Scout Headquarters.

Article 2: The China Boy Scout County or City Council shall be organized by three to five directors and three alternate directors. The director of the training department of the local party headquarters and the head of education administration shall be ex officio directors. The remaining directors shall be mutually elected by local Boy Scout service members every six months and appointed by the Provincial Council upon approval by the training department of the county or city. If the Provincial Council has not been established, the request may be submitted to the China Boy Scout Headquarters for approval.

Article 3: The China Boy Scout County or City Council shall have one executive director, who shall be mutually elected by the directors to handle daily affairs.

Article 4: The China Boy Scout County or City Council may establish four sections based on the complexity of the affairs: organization, guidance, assessment, and general affairs. Each section shall have a chief secretary and several secretaries and clerks, who shall manage the affairs of each section and draft documents under the guidance of the executive director. The aforementioned chief secretaries and secretaries shall be concurrently appointed by personnel transferred from agencies or organizations related to the Boy Scout cause and shall not be paid.

Article 5: The detailed rules of procedure for the China Boy Scout County or City Council shall be drafted by the council and submitted to the Provincial Council for approval. However, if the Provincial Council has not been established, the request may be submitted to the China Boy Scout Headquarters for approval.

Article 6: Any matters not covered in these regulations shall be amended by the Central Executive Committee upon submission by the China Boy Scout Commander.

Article 7: These regulations shall be implemented upon approval by the Standing Committee of the Central Executive Committee after submission by the China Boy Scout Commander.

(5) Organizational Regulations of the China Boy Scout Overseas Council 96

Article 1: In each general branch or directly affiliated branch where three or more China Boy Scout troops have been established, the troop leaders may jointly petition the China Boy Scout Commander to organize a China Boy Scout council, named the China Boy Scout [Name of Location] Council, to execute the orders of the China Boy Scout Headquarters and handle matters such as the organization, guidance, and assessment of local Boy Scouts.

Article 2: The Overseas China Boy Scout Council shall be organized by three to five directors and three alternate directors. The training committee member of the local party headquarters and the local consul or education administration commissioner shall be ex officio directors. The remaining directors shall be mutually elected by local Boy Scout service members every year and appointed by the China Boy Scout Commander upon approval by the training committee member.

Article 3: The Overseas China Boy Scout Council shall have three executive directors, who shall be mutually elected by the directors to organize an executive meeting to handle daily affairs.

Article 4: The Overseas China Boy Scout Council shall have a secretary who shall execute council affairs under the guidance of the executive directors.

Article 5: The Overseas China Boy Scout Council may establish four sections based on the complexity of the affairs: organization, guidance, assessment, and general affairs. Each section shall have a chief secretary and several secretaries and clerks, who shall manage the affairs of each section and draft documents under the guidance of the executive directors and the secretary. The aforementioned chief secretaries and secretaries shall be concurrently appointed by personnel transferred from agencies or organizations related to the Boy Scout cause and shall not be paid.

Article 6: The detailed rules of procedure for the Overseas China Boy Scout Council shall be drafted by the council and submitted to the China Boy Scout Headquarters for approval.

Article 7: Any matters not covered in these regulations shall be amended by the Central Executive Committee upon submission by the China Boy Scout Commander.

Article 8: These regulations shall be implemented upon approval by the Standing Committee of the Central Executive Committee after submission by the China Boy Scout Commander. (End)

Jiangsu Province Will 97

Hold Examinations for County Education Bureau Directors (Continued)

Provisional Regulations for Examination of County Education Bureau Directors in Jiangsu Province

Article 1: Before the implementation of the central examination law, Jiangsu Province shall conduct examinations for county education bureau directors in accordance with the provisions of these regulations.

Article 2: Any person, regardless of gender, who possesses one of the following qualifications and obtains a reliable guarantee may apply for the examination for county education bureau director:

A. Graduates of the education department of a university, normal university, or higher normal school who have served in an educational position for one year or more.

B. Graduates of a normal school undergraduate program or senior high school normal program who have served in a local educational position for three years or more.

C. Graduates of a university or specialized school who have served in a local educational position for three years or more.

Private schools must be registered with the Ministry of Education.

Article 3: Persons with any of the following circumstances shall not be allowed to take the examination for county education bureau director:

1. Those who have been proven to have engaged in counter-revolutionary activities.

2. Those who have been deprived of or suspended from public rights and have not yet been reinstated.

3. Those who have embezzled public funds and have not yet repaid the state.

4. Those who have been punished for corruption.

5. Those who have been declared bankrupt and have not yet been reinstated.

6. Those who smoke opium or other substitutes.

Article 4: The examination shall consist of a first examination in Chinese and the principles of the Chinese Nationalist Party, a second examination in educational theory, practical educational problems, current educational laws, and the general situation of education in Jiangsu Province, and a third examination in oral examination, academic review, and physical examination.

Article 5: The examination for education bureau directors shall be conducted by an examination committee, which shall be organized as follows:

1. One chairman of the examination committee

2. One vice-chairman

3. Three to five members of the examination committee

Article 6: The chairman of the examination committee shall be concurrently held by the chairman of the provincial government, and the vice-chairman shall be concurrently held by the director of the education department.

Article 7: The members of the examination committee shall be nominated by the chairman from the following personnel and submitted to the provincial government for submission to the Executive Yuan for transfer to the Examination Yuan for approval:

1. Professors or associate professors of national universities and private universities registered with the Ministry of Education.

2. Other experts with rich educational knowledge and experience.

3. Members of the Jiangsu Provincial Party Headquarters or the provincial government.

Article 8: The Examination Committee shall appoint a number of assistant examiners to assist the examiners in managing the grading and other examination affairs.

Article 9: The assistant examiners shall be selected by the chairman from the following personnel:

A. Officials above the rank of Recommending Appointment in the Provincial Government.

B. Those who have the qualifications stipulated in Clauses 1 and 2 of Article 7.

Article 10: When conducting the examination, the Examination Committee shall invite the procurator of the local court to serve as the supervising examiner. If the supervising examiner discovers any illegal acts such as examination fraud or other acts that impede public service, they shall report to the Examination Committee or report to the court in accordance with the law.

Article 11: The Examination Committee shall be dissolved immediately after the examination is completed.

Article 12: After the examination is completed, the list of qualified county education bureau directors, their photos, and the examination situation shall be reported to the Examination Yuan and the Ministry of Education for record.

Article 13: When there are vacancies for county education bureau directors, qualified candidates shall be selected by the county magistrate and submitted to the Education Department for submission to the Provincial Government Committee for a decision on appointment.

Article 14: Separate detailed rules shall be formulated for various examination details.

Article 15: These regulations shall be discussed and promulgated by the Jiangsu Provincial Government Committee and submitted to the Executive Yuan for transfer to the Examination Yuan for record. (End)

This City

Municipal Education Bureau Restricts Enrollment Period for All Schools 98

The Shanghai Municipal Education Bureau issued an instruction to all municipal and private schools at all levels, stating: "For compliance. Recently, it has been found that some schools at all levels are holding enrollments after the prescribed opening date, which causes difficulties for both teaching and learning. Now it is stipulated that all school enrollment matters must be handled before the prescribed opening date. In special circumstances, the Bureau may approve a discretionary extension of the date. Elementary schools may extend the date by up to five days, middle schools by up to ten days, and specialized schools and above by up to two weeks. During this extended period, middle schools and above shall formulate their own credit selection methods for students and submit them for verification, in order to restrict and emphasize academic work. Therefore, all schools are ordered to comply with this instruction."

Extension of Registration Period for Educational and Cultural Groups 99

The deadline for registration of educational and cultural groups in this city was February 15th. It is now learned that the Municipal Education Bureau and the Municipal Citizen Training Association have requested an extension because it is not easy for various groups to complete supplementary procedures. An extension of one month, from February 15th to March 15th, has been specially approved.

Municipal Education Bureau Specifies Spring Vacation Dates 100

Three days, from April 3rd to 5th

The Shanghai Municipal Education Bureau issued an instruction to all primary and secondary schools in this city yesterday, stating: "For compliance. The school calendar for primary and secondary schools in this special municipality for the 18th year has been formulated by the Bureau and published in the eighth issue of the Education Weekly for compliance. The calendar states that there will be a three-day spring vacation in early April. The Bureau has now specified that April 3rd, 4th, and 5th will be the dates for this year's spring vacation. All primary and secondary schools in this city are hereby ordered to comply with this instruction."

Central University

Yang Yinpu Concurrently Serves as Dean of the School of Commerce 104

Since Dean Cheng Zhenqi of the National Central University School of Commerce resigned, it was the beginning of the semester, and the affairs of the school and the curriculum could not be lacking for a day. Although President Zhang Junmou verbally agreed to Cheng's resignation, his reliance on Cheng was never diminished. Subsequently, the school affairs meeting of the School of Commerce decided to send a letter to President Zhang, requesting that Dean Cheng be given a few months' leave to allow him to fully consider the matter, and to hire someone to serve as acting dean, in order to express the method of retaining and fulfilling all matters. President Zhang considered the presentation to be extremely complete and has now approved the request, sending a letter to Cheng to inform him of this intention. However, due to the multitude of school affairs awaiting to be handled, Yang Yinpu, the former director of academic affairs and associate professor of the school, has been appointed as acting dean, and Yong Jiayuan, the director of the accounting department, has been appointed as director of academic affairs. Everything is proceeding as usual. Classes officially began on the 18th, and all new and old students have arrived. The number of courses offered this semester is much greater than in the past, and the spirit is even more fulfilling. From the 24th, the weekly memorial service and military training will be held, as well as how to plan the publication of the School of Commerce newspaper. The collection of manuscripts is nearing completion and will be published in the near future.

Since the opening of the current semester at National Jinan University, all matters have been carried out in an extremely organized and spirited manner. This semester will include (1) the reconstruction of several dormitory buildings for the middle and high school departments, converting the existing dormitories into classrooms, display rooms, research rooms, laboratories, and offices for student organizations; (2) the expansion of the library, adding collection and reading rooms, and a branch library for the middle school department; (3) the construction of specialized classrooms for music and art, with the address determined to be behind Zhiyuan Hall; (4) the construction of a gymnasium and swimming pool. Japan's Preliminary Selections for the Far Eastern Games 111

Philippine Athletes to Reside Next to the Venue at the Japan Youth Hall

(1) Preliminary Round of Track and Field Athletes

Regarding the selection of track and field representatives to attend the Far Eastern Games, the Japan Sports Association has scheduled the first preliminary round to be held around mid-April in various regions of the country (the Kanto region has already scheduled it for April 19th and 20th in Tokyo). Then, on May 17th and 18th, the National Track and Field Championships Preliminary Round will be held. Those with excellent competition results will represent Japan at the Games. After the decision, they will gather in Tokyo for training.

(2) National Swimming Competition to be Held

Regarding the swimming athletes attending the Games, in addition to designating a number of athletes with excellent past results, the Sports Association will hold a national competition at the Tokyo Shiba Park Swimming Pool on May 10th and 11th. From May 12th, the selected athletes will be summoned to live and train together in Tokyo. The association has also issued a notice prohibiting swimmers from various places who hope to be selected to attend the Games from going abroad to compete between February and June.

(3) Preparing for Women's Team Ball Open Tournament

Japan is paying great attention to the women's open team ball competition this time, dividing the country into four regions. Each region will first hold separate competitions to select a team, and then hold a joint competition before the Games begin. The winner will represent Japan to compete against China and the Philippines. According to Japan, women are well-trained in team ball, and it is a performance item in the National Games. In the future, the national representatives will definitely be a strong team. It is hoped that female students in our country will pay more attention.

(4) Accommodation for Philippine Athletes Determined

According to a report from the Japan Sports Association, the association has received a letter from the Philippine Sports Association, notifying them that the Philippines will send a total of 140 athletes to attend the Games, and entrusted the association to find accommodation in Tokyo. Considering the large number of representatives at this Games and the difficulty of accommodation, the Japan Association has organized an accommodation preparation committee. According to a report by Committee Chairman Dr. Nozu at the last executive meeting of the Sports Association, the association has not yet found a suitable place to accommodate representatives from various countries. The most difficult problem in accommodation is the supply of beds, because Japan, except for the largest hotels, hardly knows what a bed is. The association is currently working to rent the entire Japan Youth Hall near the Jingu Athletic Meet (the Games will be held there) for the Philippine athletes. The hall is well-equipped and close to the competition venue, making it ideal for athletes to stay. Unfortunately, it has already been obtained by the Philippines.

(5) Philippine High Jump Highest Record

Tokyo, 24th, Japanese News Agency Electric Dispatch: According to a telegram from Luzon, the Philippine Sports Association held a preliminary for the Far Eastern Games. Philippine athlete Toribio broke the highest record of six feet seven inches in the high jump.

Free Talk

Laugh It Off 119

— Hai Ke

Female A: Who was that young man you were talking to just now? He's so ugly.

Female B: That's my younger brother.

Female A: Oh. I'm sorry. I didn't notice that the two of you look very similar.

A: Old Bing is in dire straits. He can barely hold on.

B: Yes. But he keeps a lot of people employed.

A: How so?

B: The bill collectors in those shops. Because he owes too much money, they have to collect it often, indirectly keeping them employed.

Politician (to a clerk in the newspaper office): Your newspaper attacked me too harshly today. I wish I could burn every single copy.

Clerk: Then, sir, how many copies would you like to buy? Let me call the accounting department to settle the bill for you. We'll give you a discount.

Bank Manager (to a newly arrived employee): I heard that you came from a poor village and used to go barefoot. Is that right?

New Employee: Yes. I wonder if you were wearing shoes and socks when you were born, sir?

A: Your son often dozes off during the day and neglects his work. What are you going to do?

B: Then please find him a nighttime job.

A Record of Plum Blossom Appreciation at the Five Beauty Academy in Chashan 120

— Yi Nong

I used to live in Yongjia for a long time. The mountains and rivers of Yongjia are beautiful and secluded, with lush bamboo and trees. Every year in winter, I would go to the Five Beauty Academy in Chashan with friends to see the plum blossoms. Years pass quickly, and it has been more than ten years in a flash. Last winter, there was heavy rain and snow in Shanghai. I stayed in bed with the door closed. I happened to receive a letter from a friend in Ouzhong, saying that there was heavy snow in Yongjia this year, and the cold plum blossoms in Chashan would bloom in a few days. He invited me to appreciate the plum blossoms. My heart stirred when I read it, and my interest was aroused. The next day, I took a steamer to Ou. At that time, the rain and snow in Ouzhong had just cleared, and the morning sun had just broken through. The remaining water on the eaves was still frozen. I went straight to my friend's house. The host was very happy when he heard that I had arrived, thinking that a distinguished guest from afar had come to appreciate the plum blossoms. Even visiting Dai An Dao on a snowy night was not an exaggeration. I chatted with my friend at his house for a day and a night. We were very happy. We agreed to go to the mountain the next morning. In the morning, the host had already prepared a flower boat and invited several old friends to accompany us. We took a boat from Oucheng, and the scenery along the way was beautiful. The weather was fine after the snow, and we enjoyed a lot of scenery. We made tea, ate fruit, and enjoyed ourselves around the stove in the boat. When we arrived at Chashan, we left the boat and went ashore. After not many steps, we arrived at Gushangtang. Plum blossoms were planted all around the pond. The houses were staggered, and the stream surrounded them. Living in it gave one the feeling of being a divine couple. At this time, the plum blossoms were even more beautiful after the snow. My friends and I walked and stopped, looking at them from afar, like snow piled up in front of Mount Guye. Looking at them up close, like thousands and thousands of pear trees blooming. The fragrance was so strong that it felt like entering a sea of fragrant snow. Some were strong trunks with beautiful sprouts, some were new roots sprouting branches, some were lying horizontally, some were leaning halfway.

They were charming and graceful, smiling in the wind. The roots were intertwined, and there was still some residual snow that had not melted. The host then set up a stove under the plum blossoms to cook tea and compose poems together to record the beauty of plum blossom appreciation. Before the plum blossom appreciation was over, a monk from the Five Beauty Academy came and invited us to visit the temple. The temple was close to the mountain

foot. The water and trees were clear and quiet. The meditation room was quiet. That night, there was another heavy snow. I

and the host had dinner at the temple. The mountain delicacies and wild vegetables were fresh and refreshing. The next morning, the temple gate had just opened, and the entire mountain had become a silver world.

We then rekindled our interest in visiting the plum blossoms, treading in the snow to find the plum blossoms, imitating the story of Meng Xiangyang. As soon as we arrived at Gu Zhai Tang, the plum blossoms in the snow were even more delicate and beautiful. The newly sprouted plum branches were bent by the snow, making them even more

charming. Calling it a sea of fragrant snow, who would say it was not appropriate?

We then each composed poems on the theme of the sea of fragrant snow and rhymed them in the plum blossom

forest. After enjoying it for two days, the host still couldn't bear to let us go. We urged the host to return. Along the way, snowflakes were still flying into the boat windows.

We only saw white herons standing on the snowy beach. Looking into the distance, the ancient trees were bare

forest, covered with snow. It seemed that every tree was a plum blossom. The friends in the boat entertained themselves with stringed instruments. I have always liked to play with lyrics and tunes, so I sang several tunes in Nantianmen loudly. My friends clapped their hands when they heard it. However, I also wrote about my own frustrated and bored feelings, without caring about whether it was good or bad. When the boat arrived at Oucheng, there were already lights in every house. I only stayed in Ou for two or three days to visit old friends and talk about my true feelings. Some invited me to visit Nan Yan. I wanted to return to Shanghai urgently because it was the end of the year. My friends were all disappointed. Now, I append three quatrains on plum blossom appreciation in Ou: A touch of pear cloud hides the buildings, as if entering a dream in Luofu. In an instant, it flies and dances with the wind, making it difficult to guess whether it is flowers or snow. The sea of fragrant snow on the mountain is like the real thing, no need to ride a donkey and step on the snow to find it. The secret fragrance passes through the nose everywhere, how many lifetimes of cultivation have it taken to accompany the flowers now? The wind sends the fragrance of flowers into the wine cup, and the beauty's smile comforts the longing. How can one bear the affectionate moon in the paper tent, and illuminate the farewell in the small boat?

Dreadful Meningitis 121

— Jie Lu

Since the opening of Shanghai to foreign trade, the world has become one family. The infusion of culture is rapid, and the discovery of new diseases is also numerous. Diseases such as neurasthenia and venereal diseases are called cultural diseases. The harm to patients is already great. Last spring's outbreak of meningitis, which killed people from dawn to dusk, was even more severe than the eight major statutory infectious diseases such as cholera and scarlet fever. Meningitis is also known as spasms. Its symptoms are headache, stiff neck, vomiting, limb spasms, and delirium. Most people die within three or four days. A recent newspaper reported that a man named Jia in Xinzhuang contracted the disease and died in the middle of the night after his wedding. The bride cried in despair. Cases have also been discovered in Baoshan, Zhenjiang, Songjiang, and other places. People are afraid of it. Prevention is urgently needed. In the past, plagues always occurred in the late autumn and summer. Therefore, there is a folk saying that one should escape in June. Now, epidemics occur in all four seasons. Shouldn't we pay attention to hygiene? In my humble opinion, this disease often occurs when the spring atmosphere is at its peak, which has some research value. The disease may not be entirely in the brain and spinal cord. Western medicine's water extraction surgery does not seem to be effective. When this disease was rampant last year, there were many Chinese and Western doctors who worked hard to study it. At that time, my cousin Li Jieqing returned to Ningbo from Shanghai and suddenly developed this disease. She died in less than three days. The tragic situation at that time is heartbreaking to think about. At that time, my cousin Cao Jun, who served in the capital's general headquarters, heard the news and returned home. He mourned loudly over the coffin. He had only been married for less than a year and had suddenly suffered the pain of losing his wife. It is truly a great tragedy in the world. Ningbo is a remote place, so there were no injections. Water extraction was only painful for the patients and had no effect. Jie Lu dares to shout loudly to the world: Hospitals in various places should know the plan to prepare in advance and quickly prepare meningitis injections. Don't dig a well when you are thirsty and repeat the mistakes of last spring. Individuals should take urgent preventive measures, isolate patients, and not go to crowded places. Inject immune serum, pay attention to food, water, and drinks. Close your mouth and breathe when going out. Use a mouth cover when the 丨丨 is at its peak丨丨Various disinfection methods should be implemented. The excrement, clothing, and utensils of patients should never be used. It is best to burn them. It is especially important to know that this disease can be treated with rhinoceros horn or antelope horn, which is often effective. (Because it is a heat syndrome, most patients are young people in their twenties.) Do not mix drugs indiscriminately. Western doctors still do not know of any absolute cure. My friend Yao Jun was saved after taking antelope horn. A famous doctor also advocated using this substance to treat it. Alas, the Buddha said that life is suffering, empty, impermanent, and selfless. He also said that birth, old age, sickness, and death are the four sufferings. Jie Lu is saddened by the fact that people in the world are not enlightened and saddened by the fact that the plague has not ended. I not only hope that all beings will attack the ultimate learning as soon as possible, but also hope to contribute a little insight to show to the people of the country.

A Record of Tang Carved Song and Dance Pictures 122

— He Tianjian

Southern Winds inside the Palace. Long regrets continue. Where did the golden hairpin and jeweled box leave their pain? This is an eternal tragic story. Unexpectedly, after thousands of years, I was able to stroke the utensils used to wash off the rouge and powder. This cannot be said to be not my good fortune. Yesterday, I passed by Shou Tie's house. I wandered around the courtyard. I happened to see an object shaped like a stone drum, octagonal in shape, about seven inches high and six feet in circumference. The material was like blue stone, and it seemed to have carved patterns. When I approached to look at it, I found that the faces of the octagon were engraved with female images playing music. There was one image on each face, and there were a total of eight images when viewed in a cycle. The female images were all in palace attire. Two were blowing reed pipes. One was blowing a flute. One was blowing a horn. One was playing a zither. One was playing a lute. One was striking a clapper. One was holding a dance belt and squatting to dance. It resembled today's tango dance. Her breasts were half-exposed, and her attitude was charming. The shapes of the other images were sitting or standing, facing forward or sideways, all surrounded by pearls and jade, with graceful demeanor. The carving was a relief carved by the Japanese. The body was deep and the shape was cluttered. It could be grasped halfway. Shou Tie said that the material of this instrument was like blue stone, but it was not stone. It was actually aquamarine jade. It was obtained from a Chang'an person for 500 gold. Many archaeologists have proven that it was an instrument used by palace women during the Tianbao period. In the past, Yun Nantian obtained a fragrant cup, and the wind blowing through the curtains carried a faint fragrance from the cup. Therefore, he named his house after it. This instrument used to be washed and powdered by palace women, and there should be residual fragrance left. I don't know if Shou Tie has ever smelled it in his dreams on a clear night. However, the thorns and cold smoke have been buried for a long time, and it has been transferred to the world, and it has been many years. Even if there is any legacy, how can it be obtained now? After watching, I urged Shou Tie to move it indoors to avoid erosion. Although it does not have the fragrance of Yun Ou's cup, if it is connected to our country, will it be like the ancient people saw the dancing girl descending from the screen? We smiled at each other, and Shou Tie nodded. Looking at the knife marks, they were very clumsy, like the clay walls of the Baosheng Temple in Jiaozhi Town. There were good points in between, or even better. In my humble opinion, this instrument may not only be from the Tang Dynasty. Even the name of the instrument is not very suitable. Only the hole carved in the middle is very large. I thought of other things, but I couldn't figure it out for a while. I am an outsider to the study of bronzes and stones. I will record its shape for now. The work of textual research will be left to the learned gentlemen.

A Short Record of Iron Heel Red Dance 123

— Xia Xiaoshan

When red terror permeated the Russian Empire, the whole country was in turmoil. The slave life of past dynasties and the inhumane oppression cultivated a semi-animalistic, dangerous, and crazy character. Once liberated, on the one hand, they were influenced by red thought, and their hearts were burning with the idea of revenge, making them easily become dangerous people. On the other hand, they were baptized by traditional ideas and possessed the simple nature of primitive times, making it easy for them to make great sacrifices. (The Red Dance of Iron Heel) (HE Red Dance) is a magnificent drama depicting a farm girl in our country's revolutionary era avenging her father and saving her lover. At the same time, it nakedly exposes the situation of the revolutionary era. It is pitiful that the common people brandish white blades and shed red blood, only to create merit for a few people. It is sad and lamentable. The poison of the Red Party and the extravagance of the aristocracy are presented to our audience without reservation. The heroine is Dorothy Del Rio, and the hero is Charles Farrell, both of whom are famous stars. It is heard that the film will be released at the Paris Grand Theater on the 26th of this month. My friend Yang Minshi has also published a special issue for it. The copper pictures and texts are dazzling and extremely impressive.

New Overseas Inventions 124

— Guo Xin

A correspondent in London reported in January that Dr. Ivan Loring, Professor of Electrical Engineering at the Royal College of Engineering in England, recently displayed all his newly invented electrical appliances in the college's testing laboratory for public viewing. Among them, the most amazing thing is a camera that uses brain thought as its action. The doctor's intention in inventing this machine is to facilitate future courts in studying criminals, saving the trouble of general evidence. All that is needed is to use this machine to photograph their past thoughts on the screen one by one, so that the perpetrators have no way to argue. The method uses a kind of current that passes through the palms of the perpetrator's hands. Both ends are inserted into the machine box. Opposite the machine box is a cloth curtain. Whenever the perpetrator has a thought, it can be collected by the machine box and mapped onto the cloth curtain, as clear as the palm of one's hand. According to the doctor, although this machine box has been completed, it is not yet perfect. After one or two years of intensive research, it can be put on the market. People say that after this machine is completed, it will be no less than an electric Holmes.

Local News

Director of the Two Railway Administrations 144

Liu Weichi Takes Office Yesterday

Publishes Opinions on Reorganizing the Two Railways

Since the former Director of the Beijing-Shanghai and Shanghai-Hangzhou Railway Administrations, Hu Jixian, was transferred to the ministry, the Ministry of Railways immediately appointed the Director of Business Affairs, Liu Weichi (Zi Weisheng), to succeed him in managing the affairs of the two railway administrations. Mr. Liu came to Shanghai from Beijing a few days ago, and took the oath of office at the railway administration at 10 am yesterday. The Ministry of Railways specially sent Vice Minister Li Zhaohuan to Shanghai to supervise the oath, and delivered a training speech. Director Liu has specific measures for reorganizing the two railways. He will also pay attention to internal management, rectify long-standing malpractices, save money in economic terms, and strive for progress in business terms, so as to achieve the fundamental purpose of increasing revenue and reducing expenditure. As for the two items of passenger and freight transportation, which are most related to the revenue of the railway administration, they will be gradually improved, so that passengers can get peace of mind on their travels, and the railway administration can get economic relief. The following is a verbatim record of Director Liu's reply when he took office, (Today, I was ordered by Minister Sun of the Ministry of Railways to concurrently manage the Beijing-Shanghai and Shanghai-Hangzhou-Ningbo railways. I am very grateful to Vice Minister Li for supervising the oath and giving guidance, and to all the guests, comrades and colleagues for their presence. I can only adhere to the policy set by the ministry, and use people and administration, all based on business principles as the standard. All colleagues can rest assured to work, and I will never misuse a single person. I will now contribute one or two points that should be paid attention to as follows, (1) Improve the spirit of management. The Shanghai Railway was purely built with debt from the Sino-British Company and British engineers, while the Shanghai-Hangzhou-Ningbo Railway was built by Chinese capital and Chinese engineers. Later, due to the relationship of borrowing, it was also managed by the Sino-British Company. The two railways were completed in 1908. Its construction engineering and equipment are better than other railways, and the military impact is also lighter than other railways. Since the establishment of the Ministry of Railways, the restrictions imposed by creditors have been gradually lifted. Hu Sizhang and others have also reorganized it, and there has been progress. However, because the power of management was in the hands of foreigners before, the personnel in the bureau were limited by the environment, and developed a kind of withered and slack atmosphere. Everything followed the old ways and shirked responsibility, Mr. Liu Weichi's small shadow

unwilling to make any claims, lacking a spirit of courage, we must know that the revolutionary government is progressive, and since we are party members, under the leadership of the revolutionary government, this kind of bad psychology should not exist, and I hope that all colleagues will reflect on themselves, (2) Try to save expenses and increase business, the business of the two railways was very small at the beginning, and the losses were quite large. Up to now, the two railways still owe more than 61.4 million yuan. Although there has been a gradual improvement in recent years, the expenses have also increased accordingly. Last year, the proportion of train expenses Qfte Ratidg Ratio reached 62%. According to the report of foreign consultants, although the income is better than before after the capital moved south, it is not that the business has increased, but only the freight has increased. Therefore, in the future, we should save all kinds of expenditures according to economic methods, such as machine coal wages. Now the purchase of materials for the two railways has been completely handed over to the purchasing committee directly under the Ministry of Railways. The railway administration can be exempted from the responsibility of purchasing materials. What should be paid attention to now is the issue of increasing business. Passenger transportation accounts for 83% of the income of the two railways, and freight transportation is very small. In the past, due to the lack of vehicles and old locomotives, passengers were crowded and the train was delayed. Now, passenger cars and locomotives have been successively ordered. Once the new cars arrive, it is planned to change the first-class cars to second-class, the second-class cars to third-class cars, and the third-class cars to fourth-class cars. All of them are equipped with new locomotives, and passenger transportation can be solved. As for the reason for the shortage of freight transportation, it seems to be due to the lack of freight cars and the high freight rate. All goods are transported by waterway. In fact, the two railways usually do not pay much attention to freight transportation and do not try to attract it. This is a big mistake. Now the railway administration plans to set up a business section, specializing in promoting freight transportation along the road. At the same time, it will rush to build the floating bridge between Beijing and Pukou to facilitate the freight transportation between the north and the south, so as to develop. (3) Welcome the proper criticism from the public opinion circles. Our country lacks capital, and the railway industry is still in its infancy. The national railway is only more than 7,000 miles. It is very difficult to compare with the European and American railways. However, the railway is a social undertaking, and the quality of its management is closely related to the people. Moreover, the two railways are close to Beijing and Shanghai, and they are visible to all. The people's criticism is more demanding than other railways. I hope that all colleagues will work hard to live up to the expectations of the people. If the public opinion circles give proper guidance and help the railway administration in what it cannot reach, it is even more welcome. There are many other things that should be done, which cannot be detailed due to time constraints. I am willing to encourage my colleagues to work together.

Interview with the New Chargé d'Affaires to Belgium 146

Xie Shou Kang

Xie Shou Kang, the Dean of the Faculty of Liberal Arts of the Central University, has news of going to Europe. Yesterday evening, Mr. Xie came to Shanghai on official business. The reporter specially visited Shao's residence on Jing'an Temple Road. The following is a brief record of the conversation between Dean Xie and the reporter: (Question) Is it true that you will be appointed as the Minister to Belgium? (Answer) The government has appointed Mr. Fu Bingchang, the Chairman of the Foreign Affairs Committee of the Legislative Yuan, as the Minister to Belgium. However, because Mr. Fu has important tasks in the Legislative Yuan and cannot leave the country for a while, this year happens to be the year when Belgium holds the World Expo, so I was sent to act as the chargé d'affaires. If I go to Belgium, it is in the name of Chargé d'affaires. The statement in the newspaper that I will be appointed as the Minister to Belgium is not true. (Question) What is the nature of the Belgian World Expo? (Answer) Belgium succeeded in its independence revolution in 1830. This year is the 100th anniversary. In order to celebrate, the Belgian government held a great exhibition and invited all countries to participate. Its nature is universal. (Universal) The National Government specially appointed Mr. Chu Minyi, a member of the Central Committee, as the general representative to participate in the conference. Mr. Chu has stayed in Europe for many years and knows the situation there very well. This time, he spared no effort to collect exhibits. The government sent him to the conference, which is a real pleasure. (Question) Which exhibits have been collected the most in China? (Answer) A large number of industrial and commercial products have been collected and shipped to Europe a month ago. Educational products are also very rich, which is the characteristic of the Chinese delegation. (Question) Has the date of your trip to Belgium been set? (Answer) If I go, I will leave in early April, because the exhibition will open in early May, and I must rush to attend the opening ceremony. Mr. Xie studied in Belgium before the European War and has many acquaintances there. This time, I will be able to add a lot to the Sino-Belgian diplomacy.

National Federation of Commerce 148

Electrically Requests Amendment of Stamp Tax Law

And Schedule a Meeting to Draft a Draft

The National Federation of Chambers of Commerce sent a telegram to the Ministry of Finance yesterday, Nanjing Ministry of Finance Jianjian, I have now approved the letter from the Jiangsu Zhou General Chamber of Commerce to investigate the case that our association had previously requested a reduction in the stamp tax penalties on November 26 last year, and I have also sent a letter to your association to continue to submit a speedy amendment on record. It has been a long time since I heard that the government has revised it, so that the stamp tax sub-bureaus have taken this opportunity to illegally inspect and pick bones in the eggs, as if they are afraid that the people will not violate the criminal law. It is found that Article 5 of the Provisional Regulations on Stamp Tax stipulates that fines should be handled in accordance with the circumstances. The sub-bureaus are greedy for more bonuses, and they turn to hate the penalties that are too light, and the merchants are already unbearable to be cut off. Our association has repeatedly requested that it is not to open the door for merchants to evade taxes. It is only that the various tax regulations enacted in our country and the stamp tax laws in all countries do not have such severe penalties. There is indeed a need for revision. The approval from the Ministry of Finance last year also allowed the discussion of the compilation of cases when the revision was made, which proves that the original penalties were indeed unsuitable. Therefore, I would like to send a letter to check and hope that you will continue to submit a proposal for revision, which is deeply grateful. The case was previously submitted to the Department of the Ministry of Finance, and the approval No. 9478 of November 8, 18 was received, and the case will be discussed when the stamp tax law is revised. However, it has been a long time since today, and the revision has not been issued, and the contractors have taken advantage of the heavy penalties to make profits and thoroughly searched, only for fear that the merchants will not be heavily fined, and the disturbance of the market to this point is really an unsystematic system. The association believes that the provisional regulations on stamp tax are mostly unsuitable, and since they are difficult to implement, the stamp tax law should be immediately formulated and promulgated and implemented in order to enrich the country and facilitate the merchants. I should earnestly request the Ministry to quickly schedule a meeting to convene the stamp tax officers and representatives of the associations to discuss and draft the stamp tax law and submit it to the hospital for transmission to the government and order it to be submitted to the Legislative Yuan for deliberation and promulgation. I still hope to reply by telegram. The chairman of the National Federation of Chambers of Commerce of the Republic of China, Lin Kanghou, standing committee members Su Minsheng, Zhang Yuquan, Lu Guangji, Chen Riping, Li Kuian, Peng Chuli, etc.

Commercial Rectification Conference 149

Please Protect Domestically Produced Wheat Flour

Abolish Tax Exemption for Imported Foreign Flour

In Order to Save Sovereignty and Maintain the Flour Industry

The Commercial Rectification Conference sent a telegram to the Executive Yuan of the National Government yesterday for the matter of protecting domestically produced wheat flour, Nanjing National Government Bank's Executive Yuan Jianjian, according to the letter from the Shanghai Machinery Flour Company this month, I have learned that the Qing Dynasty had previously signed a treaty with various countries, and imported foreign flour was for the purpose of providing food for overseas Chinese. Because the domestically produced wheat flour in our country at that time was not hygienic, it was allowed to be tax-free to help the overseas Chinese. It has been a long time since then. Taking the supply of food as an excuse, foreign flour has been imported in its original form, and it has become a major part of trade. The stockpiles in Tianjin alone are often as many as four or five million bags. Most of the imports from Dalian in the north are in fact from the vast majority. Even the special tax on wheat flour is not easy to collect. The sales of Chinese flour have almost been taken away by it, which is a loss of the original intention of the treaty at that time. Now that our country's machine-made wheat flour is of excellent quality, overseas Chinese food does not need foreign flour supply. When the customs are completely independent and the new tariff is promulgated, it is planned to ask the government to preside over the cancellation of the previous treaty. From the date of promulgation of the new tariff, all imported foreign flour will be taxed heavily with reference to the import tax rate of foreign flour in the United States and Japan, so that the import of foreign flour can be reduced and Chinese flour can be promoted as much as possible. The matter is related to national sovereignty and the rise and fall of the flour industry. In addition to submitting it separately to the National Government, the Executive Yuan, the Ministry of Foreign Affairs, the Ministry of Finance and Industry, the Customs Department, the Central Political Conference, the People's Food Committee, and the Shanghai Special Municipal Government, the relevant letter is hereby sent to your association for verification, and I implore you to submit it to the Executive Yuan and submit it to the Executive Conference for review and implementation. The association learned that the Qing Dynasty listed the daily necessities of foreigners as tax-free, which was ignorant of the situation and made a big mistake. Later, due to the Boxer Indemnity relationship, most of the tax-free items for foreigners were deleted, while foreign rice and wheat flour remained an exception. Although it was for the purpose of helping people's food, the pros and cons were still enough to weigh. However, at present, flour mills are standing in our country, and the output is abundant. The situation is different from that of the Qing Dynasty. Foreign wheat flour is already in a confrontational position with us. If we allow it to be imported tax-free and at a low price, it will indeed make Chinese flour unable to compete. Last year, the new system of seven-level tariffs was promulgated, and these tax-free items were still retained according to the old system and were not corrected. Judging from the national protection policy, it is a shortcoming. Moreover, in the past, Chinese and foreign wheat flour were exempt from customs duties uniformly. Although foreign merchants enjoyed preferential treatment, Chinese factories could still enjoy a uniform example and could barely compete. Now, Chinese factories have to pay a special tax on wheat flour, and foreign flour imported in large quantities from the north and the south has not been able to set up a place to collect additional taxes uniformly during the transit. Therefore, Chinese and foreign wheat flour already have an unbalanced situation. If there is no place to remedy the situation by uniformly collecting customs duties, it is difficult for Chinese factories to support themselves and it is difficult to survive. According to the letter, the letter should be sent to the bank to check and approve the request of the association to cancel the tax-free system for imported foreign wheat flour and determine the import tax rate with reference to the current tax system of various countries in order to save sovereignty and maintain the flour industry. Customs autonomy and most countries have already concluded an agreement, then the listing of tax-free items into taxable items is naturally the effect of the national autonomous power, and there seems to be no need to go through negotiation procedures. I implore you to approve the implementation, which is for public convenience. The Shanghai Special Municipal Chamber of Commerce Group Consolidation Committee Kouchang.

The Flourishing of Foreign Merchants' Shipping on the Yangtze River 153

The Flourishing of Foreign Steamship Business: In the past ten days, the Yangtze River foreign steamships of the three companies, Butterfield & Swire, Jardine Matheson, and Nissin Kisen, have seen an extraordinary flourishing of their import and export business. Butterfield & Swire's Yangtze River ships, including the upper Yangtze River steamers, have increased to eight or nine sailings per week. Nissin Kisen has also increased to nine sailings. Jardine Matheson can operate six sailings. In addition, ships like the China Merchants Steam Navigation Company’s "Xiangtai" and "Jiejiang" are also fiercely competing to transport passengers and cargo upstream. Since the 21st of this month, the outbound cargo of various foreign steamships on the Yangtze River has become even more congested. Almost every ship leaving is fully loaded. Cargo arriving later has to be refused clearance. Each sailing's freight revenue exceeds one thousand taels of silver, and each company is overjoyed.

Upstream Navigation Blocked Again: This year, navigation on the upper Yangtze River began about a month earlier than in previous years. A decade ago, the water level in areas like Yichang, Shashi, and Changsha had already risen above nine feet. But within the past week, drafts of thirteen feet were recorded. Therefore, the Sichuan and Hunan merchants wired Shanghai in succession to request goods. British and Japanese shipping merchants have also dispatched ships such as "Wanliu," "Wantong," "Pinghe," "Jiahe," and "Wuling" to transport goods. Yesterday, the companies received telegrams from Hankou stating that the upper Yangtze River water level had suddenly dropped sharply starting from the 20th. Ships sailing from Shanghai to Yichang, Shashi, and the Xiang River were all blocked in Hankou and unable to proceed. Yesterday, the various shipping companies in Shanghai wired their Hankou branches to quickly dispatch small steamers to transship the blocked cargo, to avoid hindering commercial transport.

Record of Yangtze Steamer Collision and Sinking: The Sanbei Company received a telegram from Nanjing stating that the Yangtze River ship "Changan," traveling from Hankou to Nanjing, damaged the naval pier and pontoon boats when docking in Nanjing. The company has already acknowledged the responsibility for repairs. Yesterday, several artisans were hired from Shanghai, bringing materials, to travel by train to Nanjing to carry out the repairs. In addition, the China Merchants Steam Navigation Company's "Jiangda" steamer suffered damage to a large quantity of goods. The captain, Feng Jun, submitted a damage list requesting the company to forward it to headquarters. Chairman Chiang has already approved and instructed Chen Ruihe to conduct a thorough investigation and report back for verification.

China Merchants to Lease Steamships: The China Merchants Steam Navigation Company is currently seeing a lack of ships in Shanghai despite ample cargo. Foreign merchants are seizing this great business opportunity. Therefore, the company is considering purchasing more ocean-going vessels. Previously, they had contacted Butterfield & Swire regarding the purchase of three ships: "Shanxi," "Yunnan," and "Zhenjiang." However, a deal could not be reached due to price disagreements. The company's Shipping Department then changed its plan, opting to lease the "Fukang" steamer from the Da'an Company for transportation. Yesterday, Long Xiaju, the head of the Shipping Department, signed a ship leasing contract with Da'an. It is known that the "Fukang" steamer has a deadweight of 1,440 tons and can navigate both the Yangtze River and coastal waters. Once the ship is delivered, it will be immediately scheduled for service.

Garrison Command Strictly Pursues the Culprits in the Wang Case 154

Commander Xiong's Speech at the Memorial Week

After the Wang Leping assassination case occurred, Chairman Chiang immediately wired the Shanghai Garrison Command, ordering a strict pursuit of the culprits for investigation and punishment. Commander Xiong, upon receiving the telegram, immediately ordered the investigation team to handle the case. Furthermore, at yesterday's memorial week, he gave a rather lengthy speech on the case. The record of the speech is as follows:

Shanghai is a place where Chinese and foreigners reside together, with a mix of good and bad. In addition, due to the relationship with the concessions, the governing power cannot be unified. Therefore, murder, robbery, and other cruel and dark deeds occur daily. The recent Wang Leping assassination case is not considered particularly unusual in Shanghai. However, reactionary newspapers have spoken without restraint, claiming that it was done by the government. This kind of material usage, intentional fabrication of propaganda, has no particular value for attention. However, we who bear the local garrison responsibility should strictly pursue the culprits and investigate for punishment, regardless of who the victim is. As for the reactionary faction spewing blood and slandering the government, we certainly know where their intentions lie: one is to elevate Wang Leping's status, and the other is to put a bad name on the government. However, we can analyze it from a rational perspective. First, the current revolutionary government is not the revolutionary party during the period of secret work. It has the power to deal with any reactionary forces with open punishment and does not need to resort to such ambiguous and secretive means. Second, the current Chairman of the National Government, Mr. Chiang, is kind by nature and known for not being fond of killing. His colleagues all know this. For the captured reactionary elements, such as Li Zhilong, Liang Hongkai, and recently Li Jishen and Fang Zhenwu, all of whom are important reactionary elements, their reactionary deeds are also very obvious. However, Chairman Chiang has never imposed severe punishment on them. Third, anyone assassinated due to being reactionary must have special power or skills that must be removed and for which there is no other way to remove them. Thus, assassination is the last resort. Wang Leping is just a

Page 14

common person. Although he is one of the leaders of the Reorganization clique, his reputation is not prominent, and his ability to cause trouble is not great. There are countless people of this kind. Where would you find so many to kill? Therefore, even if we retreat ten thousand steps, if the government has the need to assassinate reactionaries, it will definitely not start with an irrelevant Wang Leping. From the above three points of view, Wang Leping's death is completely irrelevant to the government. This is extremely clear. However, it is the duty of the Reorganization clique to use this topic to create a few reactionary slogans and write two propaganda articles, and it is not surprising at all. Although Wang Leping is someone the government has issued an arrest warrant for, no one may inflict punishment on him except through legal judgment. Therefore, the killer of Wang Leping is still committing a crime. Government agencies must punish the offender. Therefore, this command is currently conducting a strict investigation to catch the culprit. After the case is solved and the truth is revealed, the reactionary faction will have nothing to exploit.

Commodity Inspection Bureau Inspects Military Supplies on Behalf 157

The Ministry of Military Affairs Requests Inspection of Cotton and Military Blankets

The Quartermaster Department of the Ministry of Military Affairs previously needed a large amount of cotton for making military uniforms, cotton quilts, and mattresses. Unable to determine whether it was pure and of good quality, they sent personnel to the bureau twice with sample cotton to request chemical inspection on their behalf. The bureau's Cotton Inspection Office conducted a precise inspection and drafted a report as proof. The Ministry of Military Affairs was extremely satisfied. Later, they purchased a large batch of military blankets and still requested chemical inspection. We are immensely grateful."

Grain Commission Resolves to Promote Sanitary Rice 158

And Discusses Handling Rice to Provide for the People's Food

The Shanghai Municipal Grain Commission previously held its 12th regular meeting, discussing several important cases. Among them, the high price of rice has made the people's lives even more difficult. The Municipal Government had initially planned to order 100,000 piculs of foreign rice. However, the monetary industry was unwilling to undertake the temporary advance payment problem, which delayed the process. A solution should be discussed urgently to maintain the people's food supply. Also, according to Commissioner Ye Zhuanjun's report, the city has ordered 3,000,000 piculs of foreign rice, due by June. In addition to the 1,000,000 piculs that have already arrived, there are still 2,000,000 piculs. After discussion among the commissioners present, the large batch of rice arriving at the port is still not helping the people's food supply. A long-term plan should be carefully considered. The municipal government's handling of rice involves advance payments, and a guarantee should be provided assuming a certain degree of loss. Since the advance payments are short-term in nature, and there is a guarantee for the losses, the monetary industry should also fulfill its due obligations for the sake of the people's food security and public order. It was resolved to submit this to the authorities for approval. Commissioner Feng Liutang then proposed that improper consumption of rice be strictly prohibited, and sanitary rice should be promoted. It was resolved on the spot: (A) On the demand side, the results of the rice inspection and the current food situation should be announced to the public in detail by the Social Affairs Bureau to correct habits. (B) On the supply side, (1) the rice mills in the city should determine the standards for milled white rice and submit them to the Social Affairs Bureau for approval and promulgation; (2) each rice store should display standard rice in a prominent place, labeled as "sanitary rice," and explain its functions to promote awareness. The signage will be jointly determined by the rice store industry association and this commission; (3) the price of sanitary rice in each rice store and mill should be lower than the so-called "ordinary special japonica rice" and should not be raised in the name; (4) each rice mill should send samples of sanitary rice to this commission, which will forward them to party and government agencies for promotion; (5) the business names and addresses of businesses and stores handling sanitary rice will be submitted by each trade association to this commission, which will forward them to the Social Affairs Bureau for public announcement. It was also resolved that the Xinchang Rice Mill and other factories would be responsible for the supply, and Commissioner Lu Wenshao would contact colleagues to designate several companies in each district to be responsible for promotion. Regarding the transfer and registration of transit and export rice, the committee also had opinions, which were discussed and passed.

The Shanghai Municipal Council 159

List of New Board Candidates

Ms. Smith Must Await a Reply from the U.S. Government for Resolution

The Wenhui Bao reports that the election for the new board of the Shanghai Municipal Council is scheduled to take place on March 3rd and 4th. The deadline for submitting the list of candidates was 4:00 PM today (the 24th). There are twelve seats on the board, but there are fourteen candidates this year, so there is bound to be competition. The complete list of candidates is as follows: Three Americans, including Pastor Borden, Mr. Carney, and Ms. Smith, all newcomers; six British citizens, including Mr. Arnold, Major General MacNaghten, Mr. Massy, Mr. Scharbau, Mr. Peale, and Mr. Hughes; with the exception of Mr. Hughes, all are former board members; three Chinese citizens, namely Yu Qiaqing, Yuan Ludeng, and Xu Xinliu, all former board members; and two Japanese citizens, Fukushima and Saito, with Fukushima being a former board member and Saito a newcomer.

The Da Wan Bao reports that among the American candidates, Ms. Smith is the first woman to run for the board. However, as Ms. Smith is currently a commercial attache with the U.S. Department of Commerce, those who oppose women candidates have been arguing that Ms. Smith, as a public official, is ineligible to run. However, Ms. Smith remains calm. When a reporter visited her this morning, Ms. Smith said that she was not yet in a position to comment. However, this matter was discussed before she was nominated, and she was aware that the opposition would raise legal issues. The election is next Tuesday and Wednesday. It is heard that a telegram has already been sent to the State Department in Washington to inquire whether Ms. Smith's position allows her to be a candidate. It is expected that this matter will be resolved after a reply is received from the U.S. government.

Yichang First Spinning Mill 160

Preparatory Office Hosts Dinner for the Press Yesterday

Recently, Yichang City gentry and merchants Li Kunyuan, Li Chuncheng, Li Qingquan, Juxingcheng, Cai Yuncheng, Wang Yinchuan, Zhang Jianqiu, Wu Xiqing, and Liu Zhongchi, feeling that the city's commerce is in decline and the people's livelihood is almost exhausted, have jointly initiated the establishment of the Yichang First Spinning Mill to try to save the city. However, due to difficulties in raising capital, they have decided to set up a prize lottery fundraising method in addition to the Yichang gentry and merchants jointly contributing 300,000 yuan. They plan to raise funds from various ports upstream and downstream to gather strength and jointly develop inland resources. They have also sent Mr. Li Qingquan as a representative to visit the Hubei Provincial Government and the two ministries of Industry and Commerce and Finance to submit a petition for instructions. Mr. Li recently arrived in Shanghai and contacted the local industrial community, who unanimously supported the initiative as it relates to promoting industry. Yesterday afternoon, they held a banquet for reporters from various newspapers at the Tao Le Chun Restaurant on Sanma Road, reporting in detail on the reasons for the establishment of the factory and the preparations. Mr. Li said briefly: Yichang is the gateway to western Hubei and the throat of western Sichuan. In the past, transportation between Sichuan and Hubei relied entirely on wooden boats to transport goods back and forth and exchange goods for life. It is estimated that there are no less than several thousand ships. Each large ship requires hundreds of laborers, and smaller ones require dozens. More than 100,000 laborers rely on this to support their families, not including porters. Since the development of steamship transport, wooden boats have been decreasing year by year. Millions of laborers have switched to transporting opium for a living. Now, the national government is strictly enforcing the opium ban, and the number of unemployed vagrants is increasing. The immediate need is to set up factories to take in the poor, which is also the first purpose of establishing the factory. Yichang is located in the area where Sichuan and Hubei intersect. Ships traveling back and forth must be inspected here before they can be loaded and transported. In the past, the shipping rates of the China Merchants Steam Navigation Company, Butterfield & Swire, and Jardine Matheson were the same from Shanghai to Hankou, from Hankou to Yichang, and from Yichang to Sichuan, and were not allowed to be increased or decreased. Recently, foreign merchants, understanding that domestic shipping companies do not have the capacity to add ships, have steeply increased the number of ships sailing between Sichuan, Yichang, Shanghai, and Hankou while our shipping rights have not yet been recovered. The goods carried are directly transferred to steamships in the river for transportation. Since May of last year, the freight rates for goods transported to Sichuan have been suddenly reduced. The goods are inspected at customs in Shanghai once and go directly to Sichuan, without the need for inspection and transshipment in Yichang. This kind of economic invasion has already been implemented. Not only is the Yichang Customs equal to a fictitious organization, but also warehouses have been abandoned and useless. The laborers who relied on transshipment for a living, and the local market, are completely in a desperate situation. Although the labor community has automatically negotiated, it is not a fundamental solution. The immediate need is to set up factories to take in the poor, which is also another purpose of establishing the factory. The establishment of factories is indeed an urgent plan for the present. Judging from the situation in Yichang, the establishment of a spinning mill is the most appropriate. The Yichang area and nearby Jiangkou and Dongshi have always produced large quantities of cotton, which are transported to Shanghai and Hankou to supply raw materials to foreign spinning mills. However, Jiangkou and Dongshi can also produce no less than 2 million bolts of native cloth each year, and the raw materials needed for cotton yarn are still transported back from Shanghai and Hankou for supply. If a spinning mill is established locally, local materials can be supplied for local use, and the benefits are obvious. However, the establishment of a spinning mill cannot be operated with a small amount of capital. There are not many wealthy people in Yichang, and there is little production. Since the reform, it has been devastated by warlords several times. The most tragic thing is that the town was robbed twice during the years 1920 and 1921, and few were spared. The local vitality has been greatly damaged and has not yet recovered. In addition, the public's thinking is backward, so it is difficult to concentrate finances. Furthermore, the spinning mill industry has never existed in Yichang, so people are suspicious and hesitant to invest. All these are the reasons why Yichang should have established a spinning mill long ago but has not been able to do so. If we want to reverse this dangerous situation at present and seek industrial development, it is difficult to raise this kind of huge sum without special methods. After repeated discussions, it was decided that the share capital would be 1.3 million yuan. The initiators would recognize a total of 300,000 yuan in Yichang as preferred shares, and the remaining 1 million yuan would be ordinary shares. The method of integrating rewards into fundraising would be adopted to stimulate the interest of investors. Whether the issued shares win a prize or not, they will all be used as share capital to exchange for the factory's shares. Once it is finished and the amount is full. The money lost due to winning prizes will be gradually compensated for in the surplus in the future. Once the funds are collected, the first spinning mill will be opened first, and expansion will be planned. This is the most important measure to rescue Yichang. The reason why this fundraising for the spinning mill is not for personal gain, but because it is seen that Yichang is located in the important town of Sichuan and Hubei, with convenient transportation. If we take advantage of this transitional period and speed up construction and seek industrial development, it is a promising commercial market for the upper reaches of the Yangtze River in the future. Otherwise, sitting idly by and watching the local resources not developed will not only cause the economy to wither, life will be difficult, people's wisdom will be clumsy, and customs will be bad. The hidden worries of the future are truly unbearable. At present, the spinning mill company's articles of association, business budget, financial overview, and fundraising prize certificates, prize numbers, etc. have all been prepared. They will be submitted to the provincial government and the two ministries of industry and commerce and finance within the next few days for approval. In order to implement it, we hope that the public will provide practical guidance, so that we can see its success as soon as possible. The future of industry will be very fortunate.
