Inspection 163

Detailed Rules for Self-Defense Firearms and License Issuance

Announced by the Municipal Government

For the convenience of inspecting self-defense firearms and issuing licenses, the Municipal Government will set up an office in the Second Division and announce the inspection rules, stating: Article 1: These detailed rules are formulated in accordance with Article 2 of the National Government's Provisional Regulations for Inspecting and Licensing Self-Defense Firearms (hereinafter referred to as the Regulations). Article 2: For the convenience of those who report for inspection and apply for licenses, the Municipal Government will establish an office for inspecting self-defense firearms and issuing licenses in the Second Division (hereinafter referred to as the Office). The detailed rules for its operation will be determined separately. Article 3: The inspection and licensing procedures, in addition to those already stipulated in the Regulations, shall be handled in accordance with these detailed rules. Article 4: Anyone who holds a self-defense firearm shall, in accordance with the time limit stipulated in the Municipal Government's notice, directly write to the Office to obtain an application form and a letter of guarantee (foreigners shall have their respective consuls write on their behalf), fill it out according to the format, and send it to the Office for registration along with the license fee and the required documents, and obtain a receipt. The license will then be issued based on the receipt. Article 5: The inspection date shall be determined by the Office and applicants will be notified at any time to send the firearm they hold for inspection on schedule. If there is any inconvenience in sending for inspection, it should be stated in the application. Upon approval by the Office, on-site inspection may also be conducted. If it matches the regulations, it will be stamped and registered. However, the license should be filled out and issued after returning to the Office. Article 6: Anyone who newly acquires a self-defense firearm beyond the time limit announced by the Municipal Government shall report it for inspection at any time. The inspection and licensing procedures are the same as Articles 4 and 5. However, the place and date of purchase must be indicated in the application form for investigation and to avoid fraud. Article 7: If there are any matters not covered in these detailed rules, they may be revised at any time. Article 8: These detailed rules shall be implemented from the date of promulgation.

Bandits 164

The Bandit Force Expanded at the Intersection of Three Counties

Recently, a large gang of bandits has suddenly appeared in the Pinghu, Zhengyi, Yiyu, and Caopeng towns at the intersection of Nantong, Rugao, and Haimen counties outside Wusongkou. The situation is rampant and abnormal, occupying the area for more than ten days. The scope has expanded more than before. Several places in the territory of Jingjiang, Taixian, and Taixing counties have also been ravaged by bandits. After hearing the news, the Jiangsu Provincial Government immediately dispatched the Provincial Public Security Team to encircle and suppress them, and appointed Li Changjiang, the captain of the Provincial Public Security Team, as the commander-in-chief of the bandits. However, the bandits are quite cunning. When the Provincial Public Security Team pursues and suppresses them, they flee here and there, making it difficult to achieve success for a while. Commander Li, feeling that the strength of the bandits is weak, has transferred more than 600 county police officers from the respective counties the day before yesterday to form a bandit suppression team at any time. It is scheduled to join the Provincial Public Security Team and the water police to encircle and suppress them immediately, in the hope of wiping out the bandits in one fell swoop.

After the Dissolution of the Chamber of Commerce 166

New Unity of Small Merchants

More Than Thirty Associations Including Stall Vendors

Decide to Organize a Joint Office

Various vendor, merchant, and boatman associations in this city have been exceedingly alarmed recently due to the dissolution of the chamber of commerce branch and the Ministry of Industry and Commerce's proposal, passed by the Legislative Yuan, stating that vendors and merchants with mobile businesses are not allowed to form associations. Yesterday, various vendor associations held an extraordinary delegate conference. Representatives from the vegetable vendor branch, fresh medicine association, Jiangbei Shanghai-bound fresh pork transport merchant association, glutinous rice vendor branch, merchant boat association, book vendor branch, sand boat association, chicken vendor branch, vegetable commodity association, duck vendor branch, Yimiao Yu Garden branch, Huangyan fruit association, book vendor association, French Concession vendor association, cloth vendor association, hat cleaning vendor branch, and more than thirty other associations, totaling over one hundred representatives, unanimously elected Zheng Tingkang, Wang Lixian, Qin Boxiao, and Yan [missing character] as the presidium. After the meeting commenced with due ceremony, the chairman reported on the purpose of the meeting. Representatives then successively voiced their opinions, generally stating that Shanghai stall vendors lease stall spaces at small vegetable markets and obtain licenses from the Public Security Bureau or the Municipal Council to operate at a fixed address without moving. Brokers and boatmen have fixed markets and communication addresses, but their capital is small and there is no mobility. However, Article 1 of the same law states that legitimate businesses can organize trade associations. Each trade fulfills its tax obligations and cannot be considered an informal merchant. Small-capital merchants are the most suffering and oppressed class, and under the clear light of day, they cannot be without organizational structures. Thereupon, the following resolutions were passed: (1) issue a declaration, (2) petition the central government, the municipal party headquarters, and the municipal social bureau for relief, (3) organize a joint office named the Shanghai Special Municipality Thirty-odd Trade Association Joint Office, with a temporary communication address at No. 1, Tongchun Lane, Qing Street, Nine Acres, (4) each association shall appoint one representative as an officer of the joint office, (5) the first representative meeting will be held at 2 PM on the 26th at the temporary communication address to discuss progress.

According to the Guowen News Agency, the China Merchant Tobacco Company held an extraordinary shareholders' meeting yesterday to discuss important company matters. Then, accounting consultant Jiang Xinzhao, a certified public accountant, reported on the results of the audit. Finally, the resolutions were discussed. (2) The current manager Song Yue should be ordered to personally go to the factory within two days to be responsible for handling the handover procedures, otherwise a warning will be issued according to law. The meeting adjourned after the resolutions were passed.

Records of Contemporary Figures 168

Finance Minister Song Ziwen, Industry and Commerce Minister Kong Xiangxi, and Shanghai-Songhu Garrison Commander Xiong Shihui all took the night train to Beijing last night.

Change of Leadership at the Wusong Sand Dredging Boat Bureau 169

Scheduled Takeover

Du Chun, Director of the Wusong Sand Dredging Boat Inspection Bureau, has been assigned to another post. The vacancy will be filled by Shen Fusheng, appointed by the Jiangsu Provincial Department of Finance. Shen will take over on March 1st. Mr. Shen is a native of Shaoxing, Zhejiang, 52 years old, and has served as Speaker of the Zhejiang Provincial Assembly.

Increasing and Modifying Docks 170

Warehouse Guarantee Payment Measures

Shipping Companies' Request Not Approved by the Municipal Government

The Special Municipal Government previously ordered the Finance, Port Affairs, and Land Bureaus to temporarily implement measures for increasing and modifying the payment of guarantee deposits for the use of docks and warehouses. After the Finance and Port Affairs Bureaus convened a meeting of various shipping companies, they submitted a request to the Municipal Government for verification. The request concerned the joint submission of a case. The Municipal Government's Instruction No. 1527 stated that the proposed "Provisional Regulations for the Payment of Guarantee Deposits for the Use of Docks and Warehouses in the Shanghai Special Municipality" had been resolved by the 130th Municipal Conference. Article 6 of the original proposal, regarding whether to stipulate the total amount of the guarantee and Article 7 regarding whether the guarantee deposit should bear interest or whether the interest rate should be appropriately reduced, should be handled through joint consultation between the Director of the Port Affairs Bureau and the Director of the Finance Bureau, with full authority, and reported to the Mayor for approval at any time. Therefore, the instruction was recorded and issued to the bureau. In addition to issuing separate instructions, the bureaus were ordered to comply. The original proposal was copied and issued. In compliance with this, the Port Affairs Bureau and the Finance Bureau convened a meeting with representatives of major shipping companies at the Public Service Club to discuss the total amount of the guarantee and the interest rate. After repeated research, it was agreed that the total amount of the guarantee would be 70,000 silver dollars, with an annual interest rate of 5%. In addition, regarding the term of use, it was slightly modified based on the period stipulated by the Land Bureau for leasing public land, stipulating that it should not exceed fifteen years, but could be applied for to continue for fifteen years after the expiration to facilitate and demonstrate restrictions. The Provisional Regulations were implemented in accordance with the above-mentioned agreed-upon measures, which were amended separately. Subsequently, because the allocation and acknowledgement of the guarantee amount by the shipping companies was not easily determined at one time, and the docks and warehouses were related to the public land along the riverbanks, on the 15th of this month, the Finance Bureau, Land Bureau, and Port Affairs Bureau convened a meeting with shipping company representatives at the Port Affairs Bureau to discuss the distribution of dock and warehouse land and allocate the amount of the guarantee deposit. Shipping companies such as Sanbei Company, etc., acknowledged the amount of the guarantee deposit according to the above-mentioned agreement and paid it in three installments, and a draft contract was signed. As for the Provisional Regulations for Guarantee Deposits, the above-mentioned amended measures remained unchanged. However, the shipping companies argued that the burden of the guarantee amount was too high, and the original regulations stipulated that 50% would be returned in five years. They requested that it be changed to 70% returned in seven years. The bureaus considered that since the regulations had already been stipulated, they dared not make a decision on their own, and humbly requested that the government consider the difficulties of the merchants and approve the request. After the Mayor received the report and reviewed it, he found that the amended measures were sound, but did not approve the shipping companies' request to change the guarantee deposit from 50% returned in five years to 70% returned in seven years, and ordered the bureau to comply.

Labor Union News 172

Seamen's General Union: Established on February 28, 1920, at that time it received a secret order from the Premier to demand wage increases from the capitalists and to assist the May 30th Massacre. Successively, more than 160,000 seamen participated in the National Revolutionary Movement after returning from the Hong Kong general strike, resisted imperial capitalism, sacrificed and struggled greatly, and therefore received special permission from the Premier to provide political and economic support. Thus, the (China Seamen's Industrial Federation) was organized in Hong Kong. This name was personally determined by the Premier, and former National Assembly member Wang Fu was appointed as the military representative to guide the establishment. It was a major commemoration. The General Union had previously presented a request to the central government and the Ministry of Industry and Commerce of the National Government for approval to hold a celebration. Now, on the occasion of the 10th anniversary, preparations have been made to hold a commemorative meeting to celebrate.

Page 15

Local News

Chen Tianxi Released from Captivity

Hostage Hidden in Sanlintang Town

Search for Kidnappers at Jintai Hotel

Mr. Chen Recounts Negotiating Price with Kidnappers

Detectives Bravely Capture Kidnappers in the Rain

The case of Chen Tianxi, Municipal Commissioner of the Shanghai Special Municipality and native place fellowman, who was kidnapped in the Huangpu River, was solved by the Shanghai Municipal Police Bureau's Detective Squad yesterday morning in Sanlintang, Pudong. The hostage was rescued on the spot, and six male and female kidnappers were captured. When the arrest was made, the hostage was in danger of being killed. The details of the investigation are reported below:

Buying Supplies: Since the news of Mr. Chen's kidnapping in the Huangpu River on the night of the 20th of this month, all of Shanghai has been shocked. Details have been repeatedly reported in this newspaper. At that time, Police Chief Yuan Liang issued a large reward and instructed his subordinates to solve the case within ten days. Detective Squad Chief Qiao Songsheng immediately secretly instructed his subordinates to conduct a strict investigation. At the same time, he purchased supplies and spared no effort. Unexpectedly, the night before last, Chief Qiao received a secret report from an informant that a major suspect in the case was hiding in Room 105 of the Jintai Hotel on Fuzhou Road in the Public Concession, and requested that officers be sent to arrest him immediately. After receiving the report, Chief Qiao, although it was already late at night, immediately traveled light with only one attendant. First, he contacted the relevant police station, and then went directly to Room 105 of the hotel to wait.

Rescuing the Hostage Across the River: Chief Qiao urgently telegraphed Deputy Squad Leader Lu Ying to lead a large number of detectives, including Zhang Guangsen, Fu Zhengcai, Qi Haitan, Shan Bin, Wang Yao, Gu Liancheng, Dou Yulin, Han Ruisheng, Zhu Baosheng, Han Jingxiang, Liu Siyu, Wu Zuorong, Hou Shenghan, Wang Hengshan, each riding motorcycles, hiding weapons, and accompanied by informants, departed from the team at 12:10 AM, crossed the river to Pudong. It was raining heavily at the time, and the ground was extremely slippery. All the detectives advanced in the rain. At 2:00 AM, they arrived at Sanlintang in Pudong. The rain was even heavier, and it was too dark to distinguish east from west. The detectives squatted in the fields, waiting for dawn. It was not until 5:30 AM that the sky began to dawn, and they proceeded again. Before long, they reached the place where the hostage was hidden. First, the informant confirmed that it was correct and reported to Deputy Squad Leader Lu.

Close Call: The detectives reached their destination and ordered the informant to identify it clearly first. Squad Leader Lu then surveyed the surroundings and saw five or six newly built bungalows in a lonely courtyard, surrounded by bamboo fences, with ditches dug around them two to three feet deep. Squad Leader Lu immediately ordered a separate哨to guard each important entrance. Immediately, he led the team and bravely charged in, directly into the room behind the灶披间 (kitchen shed) according to what the informant said. Unexpectedly, the kidnappers had heard the alarm and were prepared. When the detectives reached the room, one of the kidnappers immediately pulled out a pistol and turned around to fire a shot at the hostage. Fortunately, it missed and the bullet grazed the hostage's left arm, only three or four inches away. It was indeed a close call.

Risky Capture: At this critical moment, detectives Shan Bin and Han Jingxiang bravely stepped forward, hugged the kidnapper, and seized the gun (a new-style six-inch Browning No. 232813). The remaining kidnappers scrambled to hide under the bed. Squad Leader Lu was at the side and quickly ordered that the hostage Chen Tianxi be dragged out to safety first. At this time, the detectives outside the door heard the gunshot and rushed in. The kidnappers were then captured one by one. A total of seven male and female kidnappers were captured. Squad Leader Lu ordered them to be handcuffed one by one. Unexpectedly, when the kidnapper who fired the shot was being handcuffed on one hand, the other hand suddenly drooped down. Fortunately, detective Han Ruisheng was on the side, became suspicious when he saw this, and suddenly picked up his hand. After searching his body again, another six-inch loaded Browning pistol was found in his trouser pocket. The bullet was loaded and ready to fire at any moment. What was most laughable was that when the kidnapper who fired the shot was being arrested, he shouted loudly (I am the hostage, please do not misunderstand), etc.

Interrogation One by One: The group of criminals and the hostage Chen Tianxi were escorted across the river together and taken directly to the team. After Chief Qiao interrogated them one by one, the kidnapper who fired the shot confessed his name as Chen Shaorong, 21 years old, from Wuchang, Hubei; one named Yang Zhongwen, from Zigui, Hubei, 24 years old; one named Gong Deyi, from Yichang, Hubei, 28 years old; one named Chen Maotou, 23 years old, from Tongzhou; one named Zhou Lianbao (nickname Erbaiwu), from Tongzhou, 27 years old (Zhou was the one who cut the mooring rope with a knife at the time); the kidnapper's wife, Tang Li, 42 years old, from Yangsiqiao Township; and Li's daughter, Tang Yunzhen, 20 years old, all directly confessed to conspiring to kidnap Chen and rob the boat. Furthermore, the kidnapper's wife, Tang Li, confessed that her elder brother, a bandit leader, was hiding in Room 303 of the Dongya Hotel in the concession. Chief Qiao, based on the confession, immediately dispatched the original detectives to the concession to go to the address with the police to arrest him. Unexpectedly, the bandit had already fled upon hearing the news.

Acted as a Blind Man: After the reporter of this newspaper heard the news of Mr. Chen's escape from danger, he immediately went to visit him. He was kind enough to tell me everything that happened in detail (the following are all Mr. Chen's words). At 5:25 PM on the 20th of this month, I boarded the South Automobile Company's ferry to the north of Bailianjing. The bandits drove all the passengers on the ferry to the back tugboat, leaving me alone on the ferry. At that time, I was imprisoned in the stern of the boat. When the boat sailed to the north of Wangjiadu, all the windows of the boat were completely closed. Then I was blindfolded with a white cloth at any time. Not long after, someone carried me onto a barge. After about five minutes, the boat docked. A bandit carried me to a field on the shore. After another ten minutes, the white cloth was removed from my eyes and replaced with a pair of black glasses. I walked along the bank. After about another ten minutes, I suddenly heard gunshots from behind. The bandits immediately stopped and dragged me to the field and lay down next to the grave together. After the gunshots were a little further away, we started walking again. Whenever we crossed a bridge, the bandits carried me on their backs. After walking for about three hours, we reached the place where I was being held.

Negotiating the Ransom: There were nine bandits traveling with me, but when I entered the room, a bandit took off my glasses and blindfolded me with a white cloth again. After entering the room, the bandit did not take any action on the first day. There were six guards. On the second day, one of the guards wearing a long blue cloth shirt told me to write a letter to my family. The bandits drafted the letter and instructed me to copy it. They asked me how much ransom I was willing to pay. I immediately replied that my family really had no money and could only cover the losses. The bandits said that they had already spent 30,000 yuan. I replied that 30,000 yuan was impossible, but 3,000 to 4,000 yuan would be acceptable. They demanded 50,000 yuan. The bandit in the blue cloth shirt said, [unreadable word] there is no such amount, and we will kill you. One of the bandits pretended to persuade, saying, we will reduce it a little, and you must increase it a little.

Otherwise, Kill the Hostage: On the 22nd, the boss, as the bandits called him, in the next room went out at 4:00 AM and returned to the hideout at 5:00 PM. Then the bandit in the blue robe contacted the boss and then came into the room to ask me how much I was willing to pay, or they would ask the commander-in-chief to not take your money and kill you immediately. I replied that I would increase it by one or two thousand yuan. On the morning of the 23rd, at 4:00 AM, the bandit boss went out again and returned at about 4:00 PM. The bandit in the blue robe negotiated with the boss again and then came to my room again, saying that it was not proper to talk to you myself, and that I would go to Shanghai to handle it. He then took out a letter draft and ordered me to copy it again.

Copy it in Shanghai to Negotiate: I chose a few names, but the bandits did not recognize them, saying that they were the masters with rights, they only wanted you to write to He Yingmei, the letter said roughly that I was in the bandit's lair and my life was in danger. Please come out quickly to negotiate and do not let the Municipal Council know. They said not to talk about the price. After another hour or two, the bandits deliberated for a long time and said that the situation in Shanghai was very tense. If there was any other action outside, they would kill the hostage first. Last night, the prevention was very strict. Today (the 24th), at 4:00 AM, the bandit boss came to Shanghai again. At about 6:00 AM, officers from the Public Security Bureau came and rescued me. This is the whole story of the kidnapping.

Continued Capture of a Bandit: When Chief Qiao was at the Jintai Hotel, he urgently telegraphed Zhabei Foreman Wang Shifu, Su Sheng, Gao Wansheng, and detectives Gao Juchuan, Wang Peiwen, and Ding Shunbao to the hotel to wait. They waited until dusk at about 5:00 PM. Suddenly, a man wearing a small hat, short stature, short beard, wearing a dark-colored straight贡呢 (tribute cloth) mandarin jacket, woolen camel hair robe, about 40 years old, went to the hotel to ask the accountant if anyone was in Room 105. After asking, he hurriedly went out. At that time, the detectives were on the side and immediately tracked him, chasing him all the way to No. 129 Yunnan Road, where he was finally caught. He was temporarily detained at the police station. After the police chief asked him briefly, he confessed his name as Ye A'an (i.e., Ye Peiwen), a native of Yangsi Township. The rest of his confession was vague. The detectives urgently reported to the team leader by telephone to come and pick him up and bring him back to be interrogated.

Order of Commendation: After Chief Qiao interrogated the criminals, he reported to the chief, Yuan, who commended the two team leaders for successfully solving major cases one after another and for their effective leadership. Before the end of February this year, they had solved three kidnapping cases, which was commendable. The Chen case occurred this time, and it was solved in only three days, which was even more commendable. All the officers who contributed will be rewarded separately in the future.

American Vice Consul

Insists on Observing Chinese Cases 173

Shops Sued for Not Affixing Stamps

No Need to Invite团to Observe According to Regulations

American Consul Meng Haite Wants to Appear in Court

Judge Zhou Xianjue's Strong Argument

Shops in the concession have been issued notices by the competent authorities and the court regarding the affixing of stamps. It is required to purchase and affix stamps in accordance with the regulations. Those who violate the regulations will be fined. However, there are still many who comply in appearance but disobey in reality. For example, Taifeng Company on Nanjing Road, Weixin Shoe Store, Shanghai Company, Yuanfengrun Candle Shop on Dongxinqiao Street, Hongshun Shop on Qipan Street, Southeast Hosiery Factory in Zhoujin Lane, Hankou Road, Tongxing Coal Shop on Haining Road, Duyuanji Coal Shop, Baoxing Shop on North Sichuan Road, and Lao Hujiangchun Restaurant did not affix stamps on the invoices they issued. The Jiangsu Provincial Stamp Tax Bureau's investigators found this to be true and reported it to the director, stating that these shops intentionally violated the Stamp Tax Regulations. The business locations of these shops are all under the Public Concession. Therefore, lawyer Chen Zemin was instructed to file a complaint with the Provisional Court, requesting that the shops be summoned to court and punished according to law. The trial was originally scheduled for noon yesterday by Judge Zhou Xianjue. Judge Zhou believed that the case did not [missing characters] Committee to attend the trial, and was about to hold a separate hearing when Mr. Meng Haite, the American Vice Consul, a member of the [团], suddenly came to the judge's chambers and demanded to appear in court together. Judge Zhou argued with him according to the law, but could not make a decision for a long time. Therefore, the case could not be tried and must be reported to President Xu for approval.

Woman Struck and Killed by Lightning 174

Woman Serving Her Aunt's Medicine

Struck and Killed by Lightning While Cooking Medicine

In Yangxing Township, northwest of Wusong, there is a villager named Wang Asheng, who is a carpenter. His wife, Xu, is 32 years old. Wang is not often at home because he goes out to work. There is an elderly mother at home, 60 years old, who cannot work. Recently, she has been bedridden due to illness. Her daughter-in-law, Xu, serves her medicine. Yesterday morning at 3:00 AM, there was thunder and lightning, and heavy rain was pouring down in an instant. Xu was cooking medicine for her aunt when a thunderbolt suddenly struck, filling the room with light, and killing Xu on the spot. The villagers heard about it in the morning and came to see it, all calling it extraordinary.

Yesterday's Execution by Firing Squad of Three Criminals 175

Scamming Extortionist Xia Tingsheng, Kidnappers Ding Sanlin and Hu Shangzhou

Scamming extortionist Xia Tingsheng, using the name of the Fifth Army Headquarters of the Chinese Communist Army stationed in Shanghai, wrote threatening letters to 42 families including Yao Ziliang, Yang Wenqing, Zhu Shenqing, Li Yangsheng, and Bao Xiangtao. He was arrested by the Public Concession Police, sent to the Provisional Court, sentenced to death, and the sentence was submitted to the Provincial Government for approval. The execution by firing squad was carried out. In addition, kidnappers Ding Sanlin and Hu Shangzhou, etc., kidnapped Hong Wen's young son in Jiushi Village, Yuhang County, and hid him in Hu's house at 556 Maigen Road. The Old Zha Police arrested Ding and Hu successively, recovered the hostage, sent them to the Provisional Court, and sentenced them to death. The sentence was submitted to the Provincial Government for approval, and the execution by firing squad was carried out. Yesterday at 10:00 AM, the original judge of the Provisional Court ordered the police to escort the three criminals, Xia, Ding, and Hu, to the court to verify their identities. They were then escorted to the Caohejing Second Prison execution ground to await execution. A letter was sent to the District Court requesting execution. District Commissioner Li Gongchen, as the supervising officer, ordered police officer Yang Deshan and police inspector Chen Xihui to lead ten police officers in cars to the execution ground. After the judge took his seat, he ordered the prisoners to be brought in for questioning. Xia Tingsheng confessed that he was 27 years old and from Ningbo. Ding Sanlin confessed that he was 25 years old and from Shaoxing. Hu Shangzhou confessed that he was 56 years old and from Shaoxing. They stated, "Today we are to be executed by firing squad. There are no last words. Even if we act like children and say more, it would be useless. Please proceed with the execution immediately," their attitude was extremely stubborn. Then, the Catholic Lu Bohong administered holy water to each of the criminals. The judge ordered the execution to be carried out. Police chief Yang commanded the police to take them away for execution by firing squad. Inspector Shen verified the deaths, took photographs, and the bodies were taken away by the undertaker and sealed for collection.

Shi Jinfu Sentenced to Life Imprisonment

Yang Tongzeng, residing at 32 Metcalfe Road, and Liu Kenqi, residing at 12 Monala Road, were kidnapped by bandits last year. The five kidnappers, including Chen Zhidat, a native of Tongzhou, were arrested by the Huishi Police. The case was heard and concluded by Judge Tan Xinzhen of the Provisional Court, and the verdict was awaited. Yesterday morning was the date for the verdict in the case. The Chinese and foreign detectives in charge escorted Chen and others to the court. Judge Tan took his seat in the Fifth Tribunal, and ordered them to be brought before the court. After a brief interrogation, the verdict was announced: Chen Zhidat, Zhou Guiwu, and Fan Xipu were each sentenced to death. Shi Jinfu was sentenced to life imprisonment, and Zhang Ronghua was acquitted and released. After the verdict, except for Zhang, the four criminals, Chen, Zhou, Fan, and Shi, were taken back into custody by the police to await final confirmation before separate executions.

Unanimous Agreement from All Parties 177

Banning the "Die Hard" Movie

Film Review Committee Held a Meeting Yesterday The Shanghai Municipal Film Censorship Committee held a special meeting yesterday (the 24th) at 1:00 PM. Attendees included Chen Duanzhi, Zhang Meisun, Sun Yongyi, Yao Gengkui, Mi Jifang, Dong Zhihe, Ge Jiadong, and Chen Dezheng. Chen Dezheng was the chairman, and Lu Haiyuan was the recorder. Matters reported: The chairman reported that the Grand Theater and the Guanglu Theater in the Special Area of the city have recently been showing the sound film "Die Hard" starring the American actress Locke. The film is set in Chinatown in the United States and depicts the Chinese people as thieves, kidnappers, opium dealers, and other kinds of base, savage, and terrible behavior, insulting the Chinese people in every possible way, and having a significant impact on our national honor and international status. Citizens and party departments have criticized the committee a lot. The committee's responsibility is undeniable. However, the committee also has its own difficulties. This city has extensive concessions and special treaties that serve as a shield for unscrupulous merchants, so that the domestic administrative organs cannot interfere with anything administrative within the concessions. At the beginning of the committee's establishment, it immediately paid attention to this, and therefore stipulated that (regardless of Chinese or foreign films, any films that have not been inspected and approved by the committee are not allowed to be exported or imported, and films that have not been inspected and approved by the committee are not allowed to be extracted from the customs or railway bureau) in order to remedy the situation. Since the implementation of this plan, all movie theaters and film companies in the concessions have rushed to submit Chinese and foreign films for inspection, and the process has been exceptionally smooth. However, this plan suddenly received instructions from the Executive Yuan on January 8 of this year to postpone implementation, and the theaters and film companies within the concessions have become reckless again, watching and waiting as before. The committee's exercise of its powers has also suffered various difficulties as a result. The reason why the Grand Theater and the Guanglu Theater dared to show films that insult our nation without any scruples this time is also undoubtedly due to this influence. Although the committee has now sent letters to various newspapers to cancel all advertisements published by the Grand Theater and the Guanglu Theater, and to notify all citizens not to watch them, and has also submitted a request to the municipal government for strict negotiations, these are temporary remedies and not a fundamental solution. Therefore, this special meeting was convened to discuss concrete measures to deal with the situation. Matters discussed: (1) How should we deal with the Grand Theater and the Guanglu Theater's showing of the film "Die Hard," which insults the Chinese people? Please discuss the case together. Decisions: (1) Please ask the municipal government to consult the Ministry of Interior and the Ministry of Education to order film inspection agencies in all provinces, cities, and counties across the country to ban it. (2) Please ask the municipal government to submit a request to the Executive Yuan to instruct the Ministry of Foreign Affairs to negotiate with the US government to prohibit the film from being shown in any country. (3) Please ask the municipal government to send a letter to the Provisional Court to severely punish the persons in charge of the Grand Theater and the Guanglu Theater who showed the humiliating film, and immediately prohibit the film from being shown. (4) Together with the Municipal Propaganda Department, send a letter to various newspapers, stating that no advertisements for the two theaters will be allowed to be published until this case is resolved. (5) Order all theaters to ban the showing of all films starring Locke (except those that have been approved after review), and send a letter to the Municipal Propaganda Department. (6) Submit a report to the municipal government, which will then be submitted to the Executive Yuan, recounting the process and remedial measures. (7) Send a letter to the Jianghai Customs and the Railway Bureau to prohibit the export of the film "Die Hard." (8) Warn Locke. (9) Inquire about Guan Huizhi in the name of the committee. (10) Express condolences to Mr. Hong Shen.

Letter from the Taxpayers' Association to the Public Works Bureau The Shanghai Concession Taxpayers' Chinese Association sent a letter to the Public Concession Public Works Bureau yesterday, stating: "To the esteemed Sirs, it is reported that the Grand Theater and the Guanglu Theater are showing the film "Die Hard," the content of which insults our nation. After investigation, the showing of this film is likely to cause outrage among the people of our country, directly affecting public order, and indirectly affecting diplomatic relations. Your bureau's failure to conduct a strict review in advance has already caused a major dispute. We are writing to request your bureau to quickly stop the film from being shown and order it to be burned, in order to appease public anger, and to ensure that no theater will be allowed to show any film that is likely to cause resentment among the people of our country and cause major disputes in the future."

The Anti-Opium Society's Opinion on the Ban The National Anti-Opium Society issued a statement yesterday expressing its opinion on the ban of the "Die Hard" movie, stating: "International forces have repeatedly used counter-propaganda to slander our country on the opium issue, such as (1) overseas newspapers and magazines often publish texts slandering our country on the opium issue, (2) the former Beijing International Anti-Opium Society privately investigated the opium situation in our country and arbitrarily fabricated information for the world, (3) the Far East Opium Investigation Group will come to China soon, their intention is nothing more than to use this to embellish the facts and implement their opium policy, (4) on the League of Nations, representatives of various countries often criticize our country's efforts to ban opium, while concealing the fact that they are poisoning and harming our overseas Chinese in their various territories in Nanyang, (5) the United States has always been very supportive of our country's anti-opium movement, and the extreme insults in the "Die Hard" movie are also a kind of counter-propaganda on China's opium issue. Not only should our people rise up to resist, but also for the sake of the US authorities, they should take the initiative to ban it as soon as possible, so as to avoid a major misunderstanding between China and the United States. Our society will ask the Film Censorship Committee to make a serious representation, and because Mr. Hong Shen is the director of our society's Art Committee, he has deeply assisted our society's anti-opium film education. He was outraged by the matter and generously exposed it. Our society believes that the film industry has reduced an anti-anti-opium film. We deeply sympathize with the five measures proposed by Mr. Hong."

The Dalun Real Estate Lease Termination Case 178

The Appeal Verdict Postponed

Oral Agreement Between Landlord and Tenant

The Court Believes an Investigation is Necessary

Because Dalun Real Estate Company wanted to demolish the city buildings it owned at the corner of Nanjing Road and Fujian Road to build a nine-story mansion, and lease it to the Great China Department Store, it notified the existing tenants, including Laoda Fang, etc., a total of seventeen households, to move out by a certain date. However, the tenants claimed that they had an oral agreement with Dalun when they leased the property, stating that renovations could only be done after twenty years. Now, the longest-term tenant has only been there for seven or eight years, so they all decided not to move, and a lawsuit was filed. The initial trial in the Provisional Court ruled against the tenants. Fifteen shops filed an appeal. The details of the trial have already been reported in the previous newspaper. The case was originally scheduled to be announced by the Court of Appeal yesterday afternoon at 2:00 PM. The tenants gathered at the Second Tribunal of the court in the afternoon, and the number of people was quite large. The lawyers for both sides also appeared in court one after another. When the time came, Hu Yigu, the presiding judge of the Civil Division of the Court of Appeal, and two judges took their seats. Judge Hu immediately declared, "This case was originally scheduled to be announced today. However, the appellants claimed that they had an oral agreement with the landlord when they leased the property. The court believes that an investigation of this point is necessary. What is the custom in Shanghai? Is an oral agreement valid? We will investigate the matter and then reschedule the debate before making a fair judgment in order to convince everyone." The lawyers and parties involved in the case each dispersed and returned home.

Ship Damage in Heavy Fog 179

In the past two days, there has been heavy fog, and ships in the Huangpu River have been unable to distinguish routes. Therefore, the incidents of cargo ships being in danger, colliding, and sinking are described as follows: The Runda Xiang ship, carrying foreign goods and factory cloth worth 13,000 to 14,000 taels, hired the Wang Maomao ship to go to the Jiahu area of Zhejiang Province. On the morning of the day before yesterday, it sailed to the vicinity of the South Huangpu River and the Mao River. The heavy fog was dense, and it was impossible to distinguish the road. It was about to sail to the beach to dock when it collided with the Chen Changsheng oil tanker that was sheltering from the fog there. The bow of the Wang ship was broken and the tide poured in, gradually sinking. Wang and five of his crew members fell into the water. Fortunately, they all knew how to swim and floated to the beach and landed. However, the shipowner Wang Maomao has disappeared. The middle cabin of the Chen ship was damaged by the collision, and the oil baskets were broken, and the oil flowed out. A sailor named Qiaosheng was knocked into the river when the collision occurred, and Chen used a pole to fish for him without success. Half of the 200 baskets of oil were broken, resulting in a great loss. The Wang ship sank, fortunately in a shallow place. The foreign goods boxes loaded on the deck were exposed a few inches above the water. Runda Xiang hired a ship to salvage them, but due to the high tide, the salvage was difficult. Fortunately, the goods were insured for water damage, and the company is now consulting on salvage methods. In addition, the Xiangji oil mill in Huzhou had 300 bags of soybeans loaded onto the Wu Gengsheng ship to be transported from Shanghai. On the afternoon of the day before yesterday, in the Chenjiahangpu River area, the fog was even heavier, and it mistakenly swept onto the stone embankment, and suddenly overturned. The hull of the ship was smashed, and the hull was horizontally moored there, with the mast sticking out of the water. However, because the soybeans swelled after being exposed to water, the hull of the ship burst. Even if it is salvaged, it cannot carry goods. In addition, the Nanqiao flower factory loaded 240 bales of Huayi Sheng ship flowers to Shanghai. In Dujiahang, a Ningbo ship suddenly collided violently, and the bows of both ships were broken. Two of You's crew were knocked down, and one of the Ningbo ship was also hit. At that time, salvage was difficult. Although the two ships did not sink, they suffered considerable losses. In addition, there were many cargo ships that were damaged by fog on the way.

Municipal Public Utilities Bureau Investigation 180

Number of Pedestrians and Vehicles on Each Road

Preparing for Improved Traffic Management

In view of the increasing population and vehicles in the city, and the increasingly complex traffic situation, the Municipal Public Utilities Bureau, in order to improve traffic management on each road as a whole, must first conduct a thorough investigation of the traffic conditions on each busy road as a basis for design. Therefore, since a week ago, staff have been dispatched from 6:00 AM to 8:00 PM every day to record the actual number of pedestrians and various vehicles in the Laoximen area, separately, for statistics. After a week, the matter was completed. The work was carried out in the Xiaodongmen area in the same way last week. Starting this week, the work will continue on Baoshan Road in Zhabei. It is reported that after the bureau completes the statistics in the future, it will plan to install red and green traffic lights on each road to improve the efficiency of traffic management. It is also understood that if the traffic lights are installed at intersections with many pedestrians and few vehicles, it will have an adverse impact on traffic, so this investigation is really necessary.

Prohibition of Fruit Industry from Concurrent Operation of Vegetables 181

The Shanghai County Government approved the joint letter from the Shanghai Special Municipal Social and Finance Bureaus yesterday, stating: "Dear Sirs, after investigation, open-air merchants in this city must obtain a license from this bureau, etc., before they can operate in the designated area. This license was previously levied annually or quarterly in different grades. Now, after considering the situation, the bureau, etc., has changed it to monthly licenses, and the tax rate has been appropriately increased. It has been submitted to the municipal government for instructions and approval, and will be implemented from January of this year. However, after investigation, the fruit merchants in the 16th Pier area have obtained business licenses from the Jiangsu Provincial Government, and their business scope is limited to the fruit industry only. How can they also deal in vegetables, which hinders the business of open-air merchants? In addition to ordering the industry to prohibit concurrent operations, we are sending a letter to your government for review."

Wu Shunren 182

Hanging Death Case to be Heard Tomorrow

Deceased's Family Requests Exhumation for Inspection

Wu Shunren, of 697 Yuanhe Lane, East Yalu Road, hanged himself on the 27th of last month. Wu Riren, the brother of the deceased, also rushed to Shanghai from Yancheng last Saturday, so that he could go to court together tomorrow. According to Wu Dazhi, his cousin hanged himself on the 27th of last month. Instead, the second landlord of the deceased, Guan Tiren, reported it to the police. When the case was heard on Friday last week, Judge Gao said that Wu Riren, the deceased's brother, must come to Shanghai to sign and seal the petition, and be responsible for the request before the exhumation and inspection could be approved. Now that Wu Riren has arrived in Shanghai and is allowed to go to court tomorrow, the truth of the case will be revealed.

Young Girl Attempts Suicide in Huangpu River, Rescued 183

Cao Linmei's Mother Died, Pitiful

Cao Wenrong Favors Concubine, Incompatible

At about 8:00 AM yesterday morning, the Gaoqiao Banggaoxing ferry had just left Shanghai when it arrived at the Huangpu River near Lujiazui. Suddenly, a young woman jumped into the river, intending to commit suicide. Fortunately, the old dock master stopped the machine and rescued her, saving her life. She was sent to the nearby water police station. According to the girl's confession, her name is Cao Linmei, she is 24 years old and from Pudong. Her father's name is Wenrong, and he runs Shunxing Hardware Store at the southern end of Baxianqiao in the French Concession. Her stepmother, Zhao, treats her badly because she is not her own daughter. If she is slightly dissatisfied, she will roar loudly. Her father loves his stepmother and does not regret the pain his daughter suffers every day. The attitude is very different from when her mother was alive. She does not want to die easily, but it is difficult to live in this kind of family. Today, she slightly disobeyed her stepmother's wishes and was blamed again. She was extremely angry and complained to her father, but was not understood. So she pretended to go out to buy vegetables, went to Nanjing Road alone, took a boat to the Huangpu River, and ended her life. According to the confession, the police chief ordered Detective Ge Changsheng to go to the address and bring her father to the police station, warning him and ordering him to take his daughter Linmei back home and treat her kindly, so as to avoid repeating the same mistake.

Autopsy of a Child Burned to Death 184

Zhou Yu, a woman from Shaoxing, lived in a house at 1 Taopeng Road, Yangshupu. At 3:00 PM on the 22nd, she took her three-year-old child out to buy sesame cakes. When she returned, she saw that the house was on fire and it was beyond repair. Her newborn child of 21 days was lying in the room. She braved the fire to enter the room, but she could not retrieve it. Her head, face, and hands were burned. She shouted for help. Firefighters arrived at the scene and put out the fire with water. Four or five bungalows were burned down, and the newborn child was buried in the fire pit. The police then took the child's body out and sent it to the autopsy site on Philen Road, and reported it to the Provisional Court. Judge Sun Yuan went to the site yesterday morning to verify that the child had indeed been burned to death. He took his seat and questioned Zhou Yu about the situation. Because she did not want to claim the body, Sun ordered that the child's body be handed over to Pushan Villa for a coffin and burial.

Abandoning a Corpse in the Huangpu River for Lack of Money for a Coffin 185

Ding Huibiao Will Be Subject to Appropriate Punishment

A female body was found on the beach behind the Ruiyong Shipyard in Yangshupu. The Provisional Court has conducted an autopsy, and the police have found the woman's father, Ding Huibiao, and brought him to the court. According to Ding's confession, his daughter, Ding Xiaoliuzi, actually died of illness. Because he had no money to buy a coffin, he abandoned the body in the Huangpu River. The police requested that Ding Huibiao be detained for autopsy and re-verification because there were no external injuries on Ding's daughter's body, but there might be other internal reasons. It is now known that Ding's body has been clearly identified by a Western doctor as having died of illness. The police were notified. Yesterday morning at 11:00 AM, the police escorted Ding Huibiao to the autopsy site. Judge Sun Yuan took his seat. The Western deputy police chief of Yangshupu Police Station complained about the situation and submitted the Western doctor's autopsy report. After Judge Sun looked at it, he said that although Ding's daughter had been verified to have died of illness, her father had abandoned the body in the Huangpu River and should be given appropriate punishment. He ordered Ding Huibiao to be taken back to the police station to await trial by the court.

Unnamed Soldier's Corpse Outside the Jiangwan Station 190

Abdomen Broken, Intestines Visible

Fresh Blood Everywhere

Horrible to Behold

At about 6:00 AM yesterday morning, a soldier was found murdered in a small ditch next to the track near the Yangqi Terrace west of the Jiangwan Station on the Songhu Railway. The military cap fell about three feet away from the body. The body was facing up, with its back to the ground. The buttons of the military uniform were completely loose. There was a wound about a foot long between the chest and abdomen, as if it had been cut open with a knife, so the internal organs in the abdomen were visible. There was fresh blood on the military uniform and trousers, which was horrible to behold. Considering the time of the incident, it must have been late at night the night before last. What is strange is that there was no insignia hanging on the soldier's military uniform, and no objects were left behind. Generally, they have all been destroyed by the murderer, so it is impossible to know his unit and name for a while. After the discovery, it was reported to the camp of the 29th Regiment stationed at the Relief Home for Women and Children and the nearby police station. Now, both the military and police have sent detectives to hunt down the murderer. It is still difficult to understand the truth.

Streetlights on Jiaotong Road near the Sun Temple 195

The Municipal Bureau of Public Utilities is Planning

The area west of the Sun Temple on Jiaotong Road in this city has not been equipped with streetlights, and it is extremely dark at night. The Municipal Bureau of Public Utilities had previously instructed the Zhabei Water and Electricity Company to lay electric poles and lines for installation. However, telegraph poles and telephone poles had already been planted on both sides of that section of the road. Therefore, when the company began planting poles, the First District Engineering Branch of the Shanghai-Hankou Telegraph Pole Line of the Ministry of Communications, fearing that the induced current would be too strong and would hinder telegraph communication in the future, requested a change of route. Upon receiving the report, the bureau immediately sent personnel to conduct a site survey and found that the south side of the road was owned by the Beijing-Shanghai Railway. If the telegraph poles and lines were transplanted within the railway boundary, freeing up the original location for planting electric poles and lines, there would be no hindrance to either party. The cost of moving the poles could be borne by the Zhabei Water and Electricity Company. The Engineering Branch agreed immediately. Subsequently, when the bureau negotiated with the Beijing-Shanghai Railway Administration to borrow land for planting poles, it did not get approval. Considering that the electricity supply and streetlight equipment in the area were urgently needed, the bureau specifically petitioned the municipal government to consult the Ministry of Communications, instructing the telegraph engineering authorities to transplant the telegraph poles on that section of the road to the north side, parallel to the telephone poles, or instructing the telephone authorities to transplant the telephone poles to the south side, parallel to the telegraph poles, in order to free up any side of the road for laying electric poles and lines and installing streetlights.

Chamber of Commerce Asks to Clear Coal Transport Waterways 196

Near Tanzi Port

The Chamber of Commerce received a letter from the Coal Industry Association stating that a section of the harbor near the Yanshengtang in Tanzi Port was being blocked by small Jiangbei boats and other miscellaneous empty boats, completely obstructing the waterway. All incoming and outgoing boats were unable to pass, and heavily loaded coal boats had been blocked for four days and nights, unable to leave. The letter requested that the Chamber of Commerce quickly find a way to resolve this issue. After investigation, the Chamber found that the obstruction of waterways by small boats and empty boats in Tanzi Port was indeed preventing coal barges from passing, which hindered the use of fuel by factories and the business of coal shops. The Chamber of Commerce, therefore, wrote to the Zhabei Water Patrol Team, requesting that they instruct police officers to clear and dredge the waterways near the Yanshengtang in Tanzi Port at any time, in order to facilitate the transport of coal.

Widow Remarries, Then Regrets and Flees 197

Ms. Yan Vows to Die Rather Than Marry Li Xiangsheng

Li Xiangsheng, a native of Funing working as a dispatcher in the Second Brigade of the Anti-Smuggling Camp, lacked a wife. Through the matchmaking of friends Chen Fengxiang and Zuo Tuhong, he married Ms. Yan (also known as Ah Si), a widow from Yancheng. A marriage contract was signed on the spot, and betrothal gifts were handed over. However, shortly after Ms. Yan entered his house, she fled with some belongings. Li Xiangsheng urgently searched for her and eventually received a tip that she had been found at the home of a Taizhou woman, Shen Shi, at No. 954 North Chengdu Road in the Public Concession. He arrested her and Shen Shi and took them to the Southern District, filing a complaint with the First District First Precinct. They were ordered to be temporarily detained separately. Yesterday, during the preliminary hearing by the precinct chief, the plaintiff, Li Xiangsheng, recounted the events and requested punishment. Ms. Yan testified that her husband's name was Shen Xiechun, and he had been falsely accused in a theft case in the previous year, leading to his arrest and a five-year prison sentence. After the incident, she moved to No. 8, Lane 4, Xinkangli, Datong Road, Xinzha. In December of last year, a neighboring woman, Ms. Shi, brought her to Li's house. It was already late, and she stayed at Li's house. The next day, Zuo Shihong and others, who knew Ms. Shi, took her to a tea house, where they forcibly pressed her finger onto the marriage contract. Afterwards, she was forced to return to Li's house with him. All of the 100 yuan in betrothal money was taken away by the matchmakers, Zuo Shihong and others. After arriving at Li's house, she found that Li was violent and often mistreated her. Unable to endure the suffering, she took advantage of an opportunity to fetch water on the second day of this month and sneaked out to stay at Shen Shi's house. Even though she has been found by Li, she vows to die rather than return to Li's house. The precinct chief, noting that the testimonies of the two parties differed and that the case involved criminal accusations, ordered the case to be transferred to the Shanghai District Court for further investigation.

"Red Dance" to Premiere Tomorrow 200

The world-renowned Russian revolutionary love epic, *The Red Dance*, was originally scheduled to premiere at the Carlton, but unfortunately, the Public Concession's Film Censor Board did not approve it and strictly prohibited its screening. Later, the Paris Grand Theatre obtained special permission to screen it. Audiences were eagerly awaiting this news. The film stars Dorothy del Rio and Charles Ray as the leads. It is a masterpiece of romance and revolutionary fervor, depicting the extravagance of the aristocracy and the evils of the Red Party, far surpassing *The Soul of a Party Member*. It also nakedly reveals the circumstances of the Russian Empire during the revolutionary era on the silver screen. It is reported that the Paris Grand Theatre has scheduled the premiere for tomorrow (the 26th) and has also hired famous American socialites to perform the "Red Dance" on stage, treating the audience without increasing prices. In recent days, there has been a continuous stream of people going to the theatre to purchase tickets and reserve seats in advance.

A Good Opportunity for Students to Learn Poetry 201

*Poetry Key*, compiled by Ding Junfubao of Wuxi, is a must-read for those who study poetry. This book collects various poems of the Five-Character-Ancient Verse, Five-Character-Quatrain, Seven-Character-Ancient Verse, and Seven-Character-Quatrain by famous poets from ancient and modern times. It marks the level tones of each word, so that beginners do not have the trouble of checking. Each poem is also annotated in detail, explaining it clearly. It is a good book for self-study. To treat students and promote poetry learning, the book sells for half price. The list price is eight corners, but it only sells for four corners. Those who study poetry should not miss this good opportunity. There is also a thick book of Annotated Poems of Tao Yuanming, also written by Ding Junfubao. This book has explanations for each word and sentence, imitating the example of Mao's Commentary to the Book of Odes. The historical facts in the poems are all cited from old canons, detailing their origins and ends, without fabricated absurdities. Hundreds of places in the notes by various former scholars that were not annotated are now annotated one by one. Furthermore, the Tao poems that use ancient rhymes are now marked one by one, so that those who read them will be able to pronounce them harmoniously. Those who study poetry should also have one copy on hand. The list price is one yuan and four corners, and the actual price is one yuan, one corner and two cents at 80% off. It is said that the general distribution locations of the two books are the Medical Bookstore at No. 121 Meibai Road in this port. Postal purchases require additional postage.

New Development of Tokyo News Agency 208

Visionary people in the Chinese news community in Japan, given the close relationship between China and Japan and that Tokyo has become an important political center in Asia, have organized a Tokyo News Agency to provide news agencies at home and abroad with communications, telegrams, photography, and all news materials, with sincerity, agility, faithfulness, and cordiality as its motto. Since its establishment, the agency's affairs have been very developed. A banquet was held at the Zhonghua Restaurant, and development plans were discussed. Huang Tianpeng, the main organizer, gave a speech, adding a management department to assist the development of the domestic news industry, and Qin Jiezhu was elected to take charge of this matter. A declaration and detailed regulations were distributed, and Wang Shiying, Chen Hongguang, and others were elected to be responsible for drafting. The postal address is still Box No. 1 of the Zhonghua Youth Association at No. 10, Kitajimbocho, Kanda Ward, Tokyo.

Fourth Edition of the Journal of Journalism

Since its printing, the Journal of Journalism has been popular at home and abroad. Recently, in response to readers' requests, the essence of the entire volume from the first to the fourth issues has been selected and printed in the Journal of Journalism Issue One, which will soon be published. It also includes a record of Editor-in-Chief Huang Tianpeng's observations on the press in Japan. The actual price per volume is two corners, and the complete set is one yuan. Published by Guanghua Bookstore on Fourth Ma Road, Shanghai.

Indian Drunkard Assaults, Imprisoned for Two Months 211

*Wenhui Bao* reports that Sadiq Qian, an Indian fireman on a ship, recently assaulted another Indian, Aida Qian, in a small alley on Seward Road while drunk, injuring the index finger of his right hand. A patrolman arrested him and took him to the police station. This morning (the 24th), he was brought to the British Court of the Shanghai Municipal Council for trial. According to Aida Qian's testimony, he had asked the defendant to recommend him as a fireman, but the defendant demanded a bribe and refused to recommend him, which led to the conflict. The defendant claimed that Aida Qian was carrying a knife and intended to attack him. The judge sentenced the defendant to two months' imprisonment.

Weather Report 212

The Xujiahui Observatory's weather forecast at 4:30 PM yesterday stated that the Yangtze River basin and the coast here would be cloudy with rain or fog due to a low-pressure system in central China. The south wind on Ma'anshan Island was unstable, while the northwest wind was strong on the Shandong coast and the Yellow Sea. Also, in the 24 hours before 3:00 PM yesterday, the highest temperature in this port was 52.2 degrees, and the lowest was 49.5 degrees. On the same day last year, the highest was 48.4 degrees, and the lowest was 39.6 degrees.

Letter to the Editor

To the Editor: According to a letter from Huang Bingnan, owner of the Nanchang Umbrella Factory and a member of our association, upon reading the 工会消息 column in yesterday's *Shen Bao*, the resolutions of the Shanghai Umbrella Industry Workers' Conference included that the Nanchang factory does not pay wages to workers and that worker Hu Zixiang was beaten and executive committee member Wu Hanfang was stabbed. Our factory's work is contracted by foreman Sun Shoushen, and the workers used are also hired by the foreman. All wages are paid to the foreman on a monthly basis without any deduction. As for the beating of worker Hu Zixiang and the stabbing of executive committee member Wu Hanfang, it is even more absurd. Not only is there no such fact, but it is unheard of. We, therefore, specially request your association to forward a letter to the *Shen Bao* to make a correction. The association immediately sent personnel to the factory to investigate and confirmed the facts. We hereby request your newspaper to include this letter in the Letter to the Editor column for correction. Sincerely, the Umbrella Industry Branch of the Chamber of Commerce, February 24.

Social News 215

Eunuch Sanbao in Nanyang YS

(V) Fasting Festival

Every year around February or March in the Western calendar, at around 6:30 PM, we hear the sound of drums from the mosque. This drum sound tells the Malays that it is time to eat. At four o'clock in the deep night, the drum sound from the mosque warns the Malays that it is time to fast. If you do not understand the truth, you might find it strange. But this is a custom of the Malays, called the Fasting Festival (Poesa). The Fasting Festival begins in the twelfth month of the Islamic calendar and lasts until New Year's Day.

The Fasting Festival is like this: from morning to evening, eating and drinking are strictly forbidden. At 6:30 PM in the evening, after the mosque's drum sounds, a starving Malay can start eating, but rice cannot be eaten yet. Rice can only be eaten at midnight. Then, at three or four in the morning, another meal is eaten, and then they must endure hunger until the evening of the next day. If someone does not follow this rule or cannot bear the burning hunger and secretly eats, it is said that this person will be punished by the prophet Muhammad. Seeing this strange custom, readers may be eager for me to tell its origin. Okay, listen quietly. I begin like this:

In 1405, a group of lazy and barbaric Malay people in the Nanyang region first saw the traces of the Eunuch Sanbao sent by the Great Ming Dynasty. Because of the Malays' own weakness, they regarded the Eunuch Sanbao sent by the Great Ming Dynasty as an angel. Moreover, since Sanbao arrived in Nanyang, they received many favors from him, so they welcomed him very much. The Malays often called Eunuch Sanbao "Grandpa Sanbao," "Lord Sanbao," and "Duke Sanbao." The chief often treated him with hospitality. However, Sanbao, harboring the idea of ​​wiping out the Malay people, often thought of bloodless ways to kill them and eliminate a group of foolish people. So, he came up with a method. This method was to starve all the Malays to death.

One day, at the beginning of December in the Islamic calendar, Sanbao began to use his extermination method.

(Last night, I dreamed of the Heavenly Emperor. He instructed me and your people to fast for a month before the New Year. If anyone eats even a little, then this family will suffer the disaster of starving to death in two years. This disaster is its punishment, because the punishment of the Heavenly Emperor is evidence that people should believe, otherwise, you will think I am lying.)

After Sanbao told the chieftain these words, the Malay people dared not disobey and followed them respectfully. However, Sanbao also had to endure hunger like them.

After a few days, Sanbao himself felt that he could not bear it anymore. So, one night, he began to secretly eat things. Once, he was inadvertently glimpsed by a Malay while secretly eating.

(Grandpa Sanbao, didn't you say that the Heavenly Emperor had instructed us to fast during the month of December? Why are you eating things yourself?) The Malay asked.

At this time, he was really a little anxious, but the clever him immediately thought of something and said,

(Yes, I did say that to you. However, I did not eat because I could not bear the hunger. Every night in December, when the stars come out, we can still eat something.)

After hearing this, the Malay began to eat. Soon, everyone followed suit. However, Sanbao's method failed again. Since then, there has been an additional Fasting Festival in the Islamic calendar.

Urban Tales by Lin 216

(II) Teahouses and Restaurants

People passing by Nanjing Road outside the concession can see at least one or a few pairs of fair-skinned, upright Westerners sipping coffee and pouring milk in the glass windows along the road of the Huizhong Hotel. Especially in the afternoon, you can see (waiters) wearing spotless uniforms, holding silver trays, serving the guests back and forth. In fact, people who have been to coffee shops and eaten Western food are not surprised by this scene. The only difference is that the same tea, when made by Westerners, must be mixed with milk, sugar, stirred with a teaspoon, and placed on a sugar-clamped saucer. The various procedures are really tedious, as if嫌 the tea in the teapot is too little, not enough to drink freely, and they must use various methods to prolong their (afternoon tea) time.

Arriving at Tongyuchun or Rishenglou, the tea is still the same tea, but the way of drinking is very different. There is no fixed uniform for the waiters. It seems that one tea guest can occupy several seats. Everyone is casual. Although there is no music in the teahouse, the (symphony) played jointly by the guests is ten thousand times more complex than the music in the City Hall. The sound of teapots and teacups colliding has a (deep metallic sound), and the sound of spitting phlegm is mixed with the wonderful harmony of coughing. When the tea master comes to add boiling water, the long-necked spout of the copper kettle is at least a foot above the mouth of the teapot. The boiling water from the spout to the mouth of the pot is bright and crystal clear, like a silver chain, like a waterfall. As for drinking tea, it always involves a (talking) element. Except when the tea is moistening the throat, there is simply no time to stop talking. Sitting in the teahouse is like putting your head in a radio broadcasting machine. There is great value in studying tea drinking and life. Eating and life, of course, need no further explanation. Generally, there is always a teahouse on every major street, and there is always a restaurant at the corner of every two streets. (Restaurant), what a magnificent name! Dahua Restaurant, Cathay Hotel, Astor House Hotel… there are many hotels. No, the restaurant mentioned here is similar to the teahouse above, and is not a hotel where you can stay. Some people say that you don't need to open your eyes to find a restaurant, because there is always a special oily smell in the restaurant that rushes straight to the nostrils, appetizing and refreshing. It is true that the oily smell in the restaurant serves as a guide. Who knows that the (natural signboard) of the restaurant is more interesting and worthy of study than any other store.

The position of the stove in a small restaurant is often disproportionate to its entrance, and the size ratio is not appropriate. Not to mention the larger ones. Moreover, the position of the stove is never hidden inside. As soon as the guests enter the restaurant, they see the most important thing (rice). So, at twelve o'clock noon, the rice in the pot is piled up like a small mountain. (Seeing the mountain upon opening the door) can be given as a gift to the restaurant. As for the dishes, they are particularly eye-catching. The dishes in many restaurants are always stacked along the glass windows. People walking outside see a huge oil painting mural displayed in front of them, with bright oil and rich colors. People with weak stomachs cannot help but avoid it. There are also whole pieces of meat and whole chickens stacked on top of other small dishes, with a great air of overwhelming the rest. Hungry people walking past the window, that chicken instantly gets into their stomach, their throat feels unnatural, and their toes are crooked inward. The function of (natural signboard) is like this.

How many teahouses and restaurants are there in Shanghai? Judging from a small statistic, the number must be astonishing. This statistic was compiled by the Zhabei Public Security Bureau. It is very interesting and valuable. The outline is like this: on fifty-two roads, there are a total of two hundred and nineteen teahouses, averaging four teahouses on each street. On fifteen roads, there are eighty-three restaurants, including beef and mutton noodle restaurants, etc. Therefore, on average, there are five restaurants or similar places to eat on each street. From these two points, the number of teahouses and restaurants is almost equal on each street. In other words, the residents' need for teahouses and restaurants is in the same position. To put it the other way around, there is a restaurant wherever there is a teahouse, or there must be a restaurant attached to a teahouse. Tea and meals, tea and meals, are truly inseparable terms.

Among the fifty-two roads mentioned above, one street is relatively the longest, so speaking of restaurants alone, there are thirty-two, and there are twenty-six teahouses. Adding the two together, aren't there as many as sixty-eight? The residents' eagerness for them can be imagined. Among the two hundred and nineteen teahouses, the largest capital is eight thousand coins, and the smallest is only ten yuan. The largest capital of the restaurant is five thousand yuan, and the smallest is twenty-six yuan. This is probably an approximate number, because no matter how simple it is, it is probably not easy to open a small tiger stove-style teahouse with a capital of ten yuan. Among them, the longest-running has been open for seventeen years, and the shortest has only been open for one year. A relatively complete teahouse has an accounting room, a waiter, a stove operator, etc. The simplest only has one boss, who mediates between the two and runs errands. The so-called ten yuan capital is probably like this.

If we further compile statistics, the interest will naturally be further enriched. For example, how many tea guests are there in each teahouse every day? How many of these guests are regulars? What are their lives like? What are the most needed dishes in the restaurant? The number of people, the rice and vegetables, etc., must all be related. In addition, the statistics of rice buckets in each restaurant, the age of the rice buckets, etc., are also very interesting. Generally speaking, the position of the restaurant is always a little more advantageous than the teahouse, but the need for the teahouse is more important than the restaurant. The former is to fill the stomach, the latter is to adjust the dry life, and there are many people who use it to kill (limited life). Among the two hundred and nineteen teahouses mentioned above, one is called (Mixed One) Heaven One. This really speaks out the psychology of the tea guests.

All branches have been formally established one after another and have begun to solicit members.

Theater News 219

Mingxing Films to Produce the Entire Water Margin: Mingxing Films declares that the company prepared to produce the entire Water Margin film years ago, but did not start due to various reasons. Since the release of the two major films Burning Red Lotus Temple and New Journey to the West last year, Mingxing's reputation has greatly increased, and the talent has gradually increased. All kinds of specialized talents are now complete. Therefore, it has recently re-deliberated to produce this film with large-scale equipment. Various characters in the film have also been carefully allocated. The entire play is directed by Mr. Zhang Shichuan and began filming recently. This film is popular and will surely be above the Red Lotus Temple.

Yesterday's Grand Opening of King Demon of Gold Island at the Central: The Central Theater declares that the King Demon of Gold Island of the Jinan Company, which opened at the theater, has been praised by the audience. At the same time, the satirical tragedy, The Secret History of the Young Mistress, which was also performed, was particularly moving. In the last scene of the snow scene, Miss Ye sang a song of lament and wept, which was extremely miserable. It is hoped that those who have not watched it will arrive early to avoid missing the opportunity.
