Women's Life 220

Urban Life of American Women

Deep branches, shallow branches, deep and shallow branches side by side, the branches are hard to compare to her.

Jade-like skin, willow-like eyebrows, loving the golden-threaded goose yellow clothes. For whom is the tearful makeup?

| | Longing | |

Mr. Mishue Shi, a reporter for the Peiping News, and her husband,

Wang Yizhi, said in his travel memoirs, "America is a paradise for women." This allows us to glimpse that the lives of American women are very comfortable. Not only is there a world of difference between their lives and those of Chinese women, but even the lives of women in England, France, Germany, and Italy seem to be on different levels compared to them. Therefore, some people jokingly say that American women, especially those in cities, live on the foreheads of men. Although this statement is somewhat excessive, it must be recognized as a vivid portrayal.

American women, especially those in cities, are almost all loyal followers of Mammonism. Therefore, they sometimes openly and explicitly carry out their activities with the mission of Mammonism. Indeed, what is called social interaction is simply Mammonistic social interaction, and what is called love is simply Mammonistic love. According to American Jars, (In the United States in the last twenty years, there have been no fewer than four million divorce cases in total. More than 90% of the reasons for divorce are due to the mentality of women (seeing one mountain higher than another, anyone can be a husband, which can be said to be the general fashion of American women today.) There is a very popular saying in New York, namely "your money that will open all doors to you." The meaning of this fallacy is that as long as you have money, you can do anything. American women seem to regard it as a golden rule. A charming and beautiful young woman is willing to be the lifelong companion of two old men. It is not known what the reason is, but it can be said that it is simply driven by Mammonism.

American women in cities, whether married or not, have only one job: to work hard in social interactions. If people with old-fashioned minds or conservative viewpoints in our country were to see them, they would definitely criticize them sarcastically as prostitutes and harlots. However, Americans do not feel that there is anything wrong with it. However, the social skills of American women in cities are indeed beyond the reach of women in our country. The first thing is dancing skills. In their daily lives, it seems that dancing must be included and regarded as an indispensable lesson. It seems that if they don't dance for a day, they feel that an important task of the day has not been completed. From the perspective of the current American women's psychology, dancing is seen as the sweetest form of life. Usually, they may wait for their husbands to go to the dance hall together after work, but sometimes they dance with other men, and even refuse their husbands to join. The second thing is eating candy. Dr. Martin, who has been preaching in China for a long time, once told me a story about American women liking to eat candy. He said that in a small town less than thirty miles from Hitch, there was a family whose husband worked as a repairman in a car factory in Hitch. His wife asked George for money to pay for his son's tuition, but she bought a lot of candy from George and ate it all the way back. When her husband came home and asked about paying the tuition, she was speechless and could not answer. As a result, an unfortunate divorce occurred. We can dare to say that this kind of thing exists in the United States. Furthermore, according to people who have traveled back from the United States, American women always have candy in their mouths, whether they are watching a play, having fun, taking a walk in the countryside, or staying at home. Especially in social occasions, they refuse to leave this "gentleman," showing that they like to live

Page 24

a sweet life and express their sweet love. American women in cities like fashion no less than Parisian women. In the past, there was a joke in Paris that a woman wanted her husband to buy her the most fashionable hat. Her husband went to the market to pick one, and rushed to offer it to her, hoping to please the beauty. Who knew that by the time he bought it, she said that the hat was no longer fashionable, because in that short period of time, she had already seen a hat that was even more fashionable than this one. In fact, the psychology of American women in cities wanting to be fashionable is even more intense now. Husbands have no choice but to surrender to the pomegranate skirt, not daring to say no. They want whatever they want. Therefore, women in the upper class of America always have dozens, or even more than a hundred, hats prepared. Regarding this point, Mr. Xu Zhengkeng's "Records of American Customs" can prove it.

Also, American women in cities generally have a diamond obsession. They regard diamonds as ornaments of unparalleled glory. American women consider diamonds to be indispensable, just like British women's love of tea. American women originally worship money, so some people say that diamonds can be exchanged for women's love, just like the effect of a magnet on iron. The most fashionable women in American cities not only have diamonds on their hats, diamonds inlaid on their jewelry, but even diamonds inlaid on their dresses and even their shoes. No wonder that since 1920, the value of diamond imports alone in the United States has been about 90 million yuan each year. There are many specialized diamond shops in the prosperous cities of New York, Chicago, St. Louis, and Boston. American women in cities compete for charm (Charming)

and beauty (Smart). Their clothes are constantly changing all the time, and the colors of their clothes are also constantly changing. Many women, in order to be fashionable, use the same color of clothing from head to toe, even down to a shoe buckle, a ring, and a handkerchief, which must also be the same color. In this way, they finally feel charming and beautiful. Because they demand charm and beauty everywhere, the consumption of ornaments is very large. According to recent customs statistics in the United States, the item of powder used by women is no less than 50 to 60 million yuan, and the same goes for perfume. This is only in terms of imports from foreign countries. If we add up what they manufacture in their own country, it would be even more amazing. Finally, let me say a few words. The lives of American women in cities are probably more comfortable than in any other country. But what is the reason for creating this situation of women standing on men's heads? That still needs to be asked of the general men of America. However, although American women are so respected, privileged, and extravagant, most of them have occupations and are educated, which is much better than in our country. Then, taking the good and discarding the bad is what we hope for the women's world.

Mrs. Whitney Art Museum in Changxi 221

The establishment of art museums in the United States recently has been remarkably active. In addition to city and national ones, those established by private donations or in memory of a certain person are even more enthusiastic than in other countries. People with even a slight appreciation for art are happy to sacrifice money to make this kind of permanent memorial. Therefore, there was the Rodin Art Museum of the great French sculptor Rodin, and this year there will soon be the Mrs. Harry Payne Whitney Art Museum. Originally, there were very few art museums in New York. In addition to the Museum of Modern Art, which opened last winter, the Mrs. Whitney Art Museum, which will open this winter, can be regarded as a sister flower. In the past twenty years, Mrs. Whitney has enthusiastically supported and excited the art movement within the scope of possibility. This art museum was donated by Mrs. Whitney personally and it was decided to convert Mrs. Whitney's original studio exhibition into a large-scale art museum, in which it was decided to focus specifically on the collection and display of modern American art, with other countries taking a secondary position.

Her enthusiastic support for art has attracted national attention, because most women engaged in art do not have a large organization, but are merely a kind of private and weak research. Therefore, after the people of the whole country were disappointed with the Joint Exhibition of American Female Artists, Mrs. Whitney's grand event was even more regarded as the first time that women in China had shown their talents in the art world.
